)@@G@@ES)^@)^@)^@)^@)^@1A@7AC3AC7A[[E-GCDIE-[^@)^@)^@)^@)^@)@@K@@=%9 CLN%- DD[EU
)@@G@@CD#D9HD(PD1DE-T^[#D-DD1D*[S@@@*SDFF*@I@@@@      SUBROUTINE NIMCGS (N, A,EV
)@@G@@ B, FUNEX, IP, NP, IS, NS, IOPT, VINT, $) MCGS0005    @I@@@@      DOUBLEEW
)@@G@@ PRECISION C, H, SUM, V, W, WEIGHT, WTP                     MCGS0010    EX
)@@G@@@I@@@@      COMMON /QUAD20/ V(210), W(210)                              EY
)@@G@@      MCGS0015    @I@@@@      EXTERNAL FUNEX                            EZ
)@@G@@                        MCGS0020    @I@@@@      DIMENSION A(6), B(6), C(FA
)@@G@@6), H(6), IP(6), IS(6), L(6), M(6),       MCGS0025    @I@@@@     1 MLO(2FB
)@@G@@0), MHI(20), M1(6), M2(6), WTP(5), X(6)                     MCGS0030    FC
)@@G@@@I@@@@      EQUIVALENCE (L1,L(1)), (L2,L(2)), (L3,L(3)), (L4,L(4)),     FD
)@@G@@      MCGS0035    @I@@@@     1 (L5,L(5)), (L6,L(6)), (M11,M1(1)), (M21,MFE
)@@G@@1(2)), (M31,M1(3)),     MCGS0040    @I@@@@     2 (M41,M1(4)), (M51,M1(5)FF
)@@G@@), (M61,M1(6)), (M12,M2(1)), (M22,M2(2)), MCGS0045    @I@@@@     3 (M32,FG
)@@G@@M2(3)), (M42,M2(4)), (M52,M2(5)), (M62,M2(6))               MCGS0050    FH
)@@G@@@I@@@@C     ************************************************************FI
)@@G@@******MCGS0055    @I@@@@C     NUMERICAL INTEGRATION OVER AN N-DIMENSIONAFJ
)@@G@@L HYPERRECTANGLE,       MCGS0060    @I@@@@C     A .LE. X .LE. B, FOR UP FK
)@@G@@TO N = 6 DIMENSIONS.  GAUSSIAN QUAD-      MCGS0065    @I@@@@C     RATUREFL
)@@G@@, WHOSE ORDER IS DETERMINED BY THE IP ARRAY OR NP, (UP TO   MCGS0070    FM
)@@G@@@I@@@@C     ORDER 20) IS USED OVER SUBREGIONS DETERMINED IS ARRAY OR NS.FN
)@@G@@      MCGS0075    @I@@@@C     ******************************************FO
)@@G@@************************MCGS0080    @I@@@@C     N     = DIMENSIONALITY  FP
)@@G@@                                          MCGS0085    @I@@@@C     A     FQ
)@@G@@= ARRAY OF LOWER LIMITS OF INTEGRATION REGION               MCGS0090    FR
)@@G@@@I@@@@C     B     = ARRAY OF UPPER LIMITS OF INTEGRATION REGION         FS
)@@G@@      MCGS0095    @I@@@@C     FUNEX = NAME OF FUNCTION TO BE INTEGRATED FT
)@@G@@                        MCGS0100    @I@@@@C     IP    = ARRAY OF QUADRATFU
)@@G@@URE ORDERS USED FOR EACH INTERVAL IF NP=0 MCGS0105    @I@@@@C     NP    FV
)@@G@@= QUADRATURE ORDER USED FOR EVERY INTERVAL IF POSITIVE      MCGS0110    FW
)@@G@@@I@@@@C     IS    = ARRAY OF NO. SUBDIVISIONS USED FOR EACH INTERVAL IF FX
)@@G@@NS=0  MCGS0120    @I@@@@C     NS    = NO. SUBDIVISIONS USED FOR EVERY INFY
)@@G@@TERVAL IF POSITIVE      MCGS0125    @I@@@@C     IOPT  = OUTPUT OPTION   FZ
)@@G@@                                          MCGS0130    @I@@@@C     VINT  GA
)@@G@@= COMPUTED ESTIMATE OF INTEGRAL                             MCGS0135    GB
)@@G@@@I@@@@C     $K    = RETURN TO STATEMENT K IF ERRORS OCCUR               GC
)@@G@@      MCGS0140    @I@@@@C     ******************************************GD
)@@G@@************************MCGS0145    @I@@@@      DATA NCALL/0/           GE
)@@G@@                                          MCGS0150    @I@@@@      DATA MGF
)@@G@@LO /  1,   2,   4,   7,  11,  16,  22,  29,  37,  46,       MCGS0155    GG
)@@G@@@I@@@@     *           56,  67,  79,  92, 106, 121, 137, 154, 172, 191/ GH
)@@G@@      MCGS0156    @I@@@@      DATA MHI /  1,   3,   6,  10,  15,  21,  2GI
)@@G@@8,  36,  45,  55,       MCGS0160    @I@@@@     *           66,  78,  91,GJ
)@@G@@ 105, 120, 136, 153, 171, 190, 210/       MCGS0161    @I@@@@      T0= TIGK
)@@G@@MEF(0.)                                                     MCGS0165    GL
)@@G@@@I@@@@      NCALL= NCALL + 1                                            GM
)@@G@@      MCGS0170    @I@@@@      CALL NIGQ20                               GN
)@@G@@                        MCGS0172    @I@@@@C     CHECK NO. PARAMETERS    GO
)@@G@@                                          MCGS0180    @I@@@@      CALL UGP
)@@G@@RXITP(11)                                                   MCGS0183    GQ
)@@G@@@I@@@@C     CHECK FOR WARNINGS AND ERRORS                               GR
)@@G@@      MCGS0186    @I@@@@      IERR= -1                                  GS
)@@G@@                        MCGS0190    @I@@@@C     CHECK IF FUNEX IS A FUNCGT
)@@G@@TION                                      MCGS0193    @I@@@@      INCODEGU
)@@G@@= FLD(0, 6, FUNEX)                                          MCGS0196    GV
)@@G@@@I@@@@      IF (INCODE .NE. 0 .AND. INCODE .NE. 63) GO TO 110           GW
)@@G@@      MCGS0200    @I@@@@      PRINT 105                                 GX
)@@G@@                        MCGS0203    @I@@@@  105 FORMAT (1H0,'*ERROR, U IGY
)@@G@@S NOT THE NAME OF A FUNCTION SUBPROGRAM.')MCGS0206    @I@@@@      IERR= GZ
)@@G@@1                                                           MCGS0210    HA
)@@G@@@I@@@@C     CHECK N, NP, NS                                             HB
)@@G@@      MCGS0213    @I@@@@  110 IF (N .GE. 1 .AND. N .LE. 6) GO TO 120    HC
)@@G@@                        MCGS0216    @I@@@@      PRINT 115, N            HD
)@@G@@                                          MCGS0220    @I@@@@  115 FORMATHE
)@@G@@ (1H0,'*ERROR, N =',I12,',  N MUST BE .GE. 1 AND .LE. 6.')  MCGS0223    HF
)@@G@@@I@@@@      IERR= 1                                                     HG
)@@G@@      MCGS0226    @I@@@@  120 IF (NP .GE. 0 .AND. NP .LE. 20) GO TO 130 HH
)@@G@@                        MCGS0230    @I@@@@      PRINT 125, NP           HI
)@@G@@                                          MCGS0233    @I@@@@  125 FORMATHJ
)@@G@@(1H0,'*ERROR, NP =',I12,',  NP MUST BE .GE. 0 AND .LE. 20.')MCGS0236    HK
)@@G@@@I@@@@      IERR= 1                                                     HL
)@@G@@      MCGS0240    @I@@@@  130 IF (NS .GE. 0) GO TO 140                  HM
)@@G@@                        MCGS0243    @I@@@@      PRINT 135, NS           HN
)@@G@@                                          MCGS0246    @I@@@@  135 FORMATHO
)@@G@@ (1H0,'*ERROR, NS =',I12,',  NS MUST BE .GE. 0.')           MCGS0250    HP
)@@G@@@I@@@@      IERR= 1                                                     HQ
)@@G@@      MCGS0253    @I@@@@C     CHECK IOPT (WARNING ONLY)                 HR
)@@G@@                        MCGS0256    @I@@@@  140 IF (IOPT .EQ. 0 .OR. IOPHS
)@@G@@T .EQ. 1) GO TO 150                       MCGS0260    @I@@@@      PRINT HT
)@@G@@145, IOPT                                                   MCGS0263    HU
)@@G@@@I@@@@  145 FORMAT (1H0,'*WARNING, IOPT IS NOT 0 OR 1, IOPT =', I12,    HV
)@@G@@      MCGS0266    @I@@@@     * ',  IOPT = 1 ASSUMED.')                  HW
)@@G@@                        MCGS0270    @I@@@@      IERR= MAX(0,IERR)       HX
)@@G@@                                          MCGS0273    @I@@@@C     TERMINHY
)@@G@@ATE IF ERRORS OCCURED                                       MCGS0276    HZ
)@@G@@@I@@@@  150 IF (IERR) 200, 153, 1000                                    IA
)@@G@@      MCGS0280    @I@@@@  153 PRINT 155                                 IB
)@@G@@                        MCGS0283    @I@@@@  155 FORMAT (1H0)            IC
)@@G@@                                          MCGS0286    @I@@@@      CALL UID
)@@G@@RWALK ('NIMCGS', 0)                                         MCGS0290    IE
)@@G@@@I@@@@C     INITIALIZATIONS                                             IF
)@@G@@      MCGS0295    @I@@@@  200 IF (NP) 210, 210, 250                     IG
)@@G@@                        MCGS0300    @I@@@@  210 DO 230 J= 1, N          IH
)@@G@@                                          MCGS0305    @I@@@@      K= IP(II
)@@G@@J)                                                          MCGS0310    IJ
)@@G@@@I@@@@C     ERROR IF NOT 1 TO 20                                        IK
)@@G@@      MCGS0315    @I@@@@      IF (K .LT. 1 .OR. K .GT. 20) GO TO 240    IL
)@@G@@                        MCGS0320    @I@@@@      M1(J)= MLO(K)           IM
)@@G@@                                          MCGS0325    @I@@@@      M2(J)=IN
)@@G@@ MHI(K)                                                     MCGS0330    IO
)@@G@@@I@@@@  230 M(J)= K                                                     IP
)@@G@@      MCGS0335    @I@@@@      GO TO 300                                 IQ
)@@G@@                        MCGS0340    @I@@@@  240 PRINT 245, (IP(J), J= 1,IR
)@@G@@ N)                                       MCGS0350    @I@@@@  245 FORMATIS
)@@G@@ (1H0, '*ERROR, NP = 0 AND SOME IP(J) .LT. 1 OR .GT. 20.'/  MCGS0355    IT
)@@G@@@I@@@@     * 1H0, 8X, 'IP CONTAINS ', 6I13)                             IU
)@@G@@      MCGS0360    @I@@@@      IERR= 1                                   IV
)@@G@@                        MCGS0365    @I@@@@      GO TO 300               IW
)@@G@@                                          MCGS0370    @I@@@@  250 DO 260IX
)@@G@@ J= 1, N                                                    MCGS0375    IY
)@@G@@@I@@@@      M1(J)= MLO(NP)                                              IZ
)@@G@@      MCGS0380    @I@@@@      M2(J)= MHI(NP)                            JA
)@@G@@                        MCGS0385    @I@@@@  260 M(J)= NP                JB
)@@G@@                                          MCGS0390    @I@@@@  300 IF (NSJC
)@@G@@) 310, 310, 350                                             MCGS0395    JD
)@@G@@@I@@@@  310 DO 330 J= 1, N                                              JE
)@@G@@      MCGS0400    @I@@@@C     ERROR IF NOT POSITIVE                     JF
)@@G@@                        MCGS0405    @I@@@@      IF (IS(J)) 340, 340, 320JG
)@@G@@                                          MCGS0410    @I@@@@  320 H(J)= JH
)@@G@@(B(J) - A(J)) / (2*IS(J))                                   MCGS0415    JI
)@@G@@@I@@@@  330 L(J)= IS(J)                                                 JJ
)@@G@@      MCGS0420    @I@@@@      GO TO 400                                 JK
)@@G@@                        MCGS0425    @I@@@@  340 PRINT 345, (IS(J), J= 1,JL
)@@G@@ N)                                       MCGS0430    @I@@@@  345 FORMATJM
)@@G@@ (1H0,'*ERROR, NS = 0 AND SOME IS(J) .LT. 1.'/              MCGS0435    JN
)@@G@@@I@@@@     * 1H0, 8X, 'IS CONTAINS ', 6I13)                             JO
)@@G@@      MCGS0440    @I@@@@      IERR= 1                                   JP
)@@G@@                        MCGS0450    @I@@@@      GO TO 400               JQ
)@@G@@                                          MCGS0455    @I@@@@  350 DO 360JR
)@@G@@ J= 1, N                                                    MCGS0460    JS
)@@G@@@I@@@@      H(J)= (B(J) - A(J)) / (2*NS)                                JT
)@@G@@      MCGS0465    @I@@@@  360 L(J)= NS                                  JU
)@@G@@                        MCGS0470    @I@@@@C     TERMINATE IF ERRORS OCCUJV
)@@G@@RED                                       MCGS0475    @I@@@@  400 IF (IEJW
)@@G@@RR) 405, 405, 1000                                          MCGS0480    JX
)@@G@@@I@@@@C     COMPUTE NO. QUADRATURE POINTS                               JY
)@@G@@      MCGS0490    @I@@@@  405 NQUAD= 1                                  JZ
)@@G@@                        MCGS0491    @I@@@@      DO 406 J= 1, N          KA
)@@G@@                                          MCGS0492    @I@@@@  406 NQUAD=KB
)@@G@@ NQUAD*L(J)*M(J)                                            MCGS0495    KC
)@@G@@@I@@@@C     SET UP LOOP CONTROLS                                        KD
)@@G@@      MCGS0500    @I@@@@      ASSIGN 520 TO LAB1                        KE
)@@G@@                        MCGS0510    @I@@@@      ASSIGN 530 TO LAB2      KF
)@@G@@                                          MCGS0520    @I@@@@      ASSIGNKG
)@@G@@ 540 TO LAB3                                                MCGS0530    KH
)@@G@@@I@@@@      ASSIGN 550 TO LAB4                                          KI
)@@G@@      MCGS0540    @I@@@@      ASSIGN 560 TO LAB5                        KJ
)@@G@@                        MCGS0550    @I@@@@      GO TO (410, 420, 430, 44KK
)@@G@@0, 450, 500), N                           MCGS0560    @I@@@@  410 ASSIGNKL
)@@G@@ 511 TO LAB1                                                MCGS0570    KM
)@@G@@@I@@@@      GO TO 500                                                   KN
)@@G@@      MCGS0580    @I@@@@  420 ASSIGN 521 TO LAB2                        KO
)@@G@@                        MCGS0590    @I@@@@      GO TO 500               KP
)@@G@@                                          MCGS0600    @I@@@@  430 ASSIGNKQ
)@@G@@ 531 TO LAB3                                                MCGS0610    KR
)@@G@@@I@@@@      GO TO 500                                                   KS
)@@G@@      MCGS0620    @I@@@@  440 ASSIGN 541 TO LAB4                        KT
)@@G@@                        MCGS0630    @I@@@@      GO TO 500               KU
)@@G@@                                          MCGS0640    @I@@@@  450 ASSIGNKV
)@@G@@ 551 TO LAB5                                                MCGS0650    KW
)@@G@@@I@@@@      GO TO 500                                                   KX
)@@G@@      MCGS0660    @I@@@@C     INTEGRAL EVALUATION                       KY
)@@G@@                        MCGS0670    @I@@@@  500 SUM= 0.                 KZ
)@@G@@                                          MCGS0680    @I@@@@C     INNER LA
)@@G@@LOOP IF N=1                                                 MCGS0690    LB
)@@G@@@I@@@@  510 DO 661 J1= 1, L1                                            LC
)@@G@@      MCGS0700    @I@@@@      C(1)= A(1) + (2*J1-1)*H(1)                LD
)@@G@@                        MCGS0710    @I@@@@      DO 660 I1= M11, M12     LE
)@@G@@                                          MCGS0720    @I@@@@      X(1)= LF
)@@G@@C(1) + H(1)*V(I1)                                           MCGS0730    LG
)@@G@@@I@@@@      WEIGHT= W(I1)                                               LH
)@@G@@      MCGS0740    @I@@@@      GO TO LAB1                                LI
)@@G@@                        MCGS0750    @I@@@@  511 SUM= SUM + WEIGHT*FUNEX(LJ
)@@G@@X)                                        MCGS0760    @I@@@@      GO TO LK
)@@G@@660                                                         MCGS0770    LL
)@@G@@@I@@@@C     INNER LOOP IF N=2                                           LM
)@@G@@      MCGS0780    @I@@@@  520 WTP(1)= WEIGHT                            LN
)@@G@@                        MCGS0790    @I@@@@      DO 651 J2= 1, L2        LO
)@@G@@                                          MCGS0800    @I@@@@      C(2)= LP
)@@G@@A(2) + (2*J2-1)*H(2)                                        MCGS0810    LQ
)@@G@@@I@@@@      DO 650 I2= M21, M22                                         LR
)@@G@@      MCGS0820    @I@@@@      X(2)= C(2) + H(2)*V(I2)                   LS
)@@G@@                        MCGS0830    @I@@@@      WEIGHT= WTP(1)*W(I2)    LT
)@@G@@                                          MCGS0840    @I@@@@      GO TO LU
)@@G@@LAB2                                                        MCGS0850    LV
)@@G@@@I@@@@  521 SUM= SUM + WEIGHT*FUNEX(X)                                  LW
)@@G@@      MCGS0860    @I@@@@      GO TO 650                                 LX
)@@G@@                        MCGS0870    @I@@@@C     INNER LOOP IF N=3       LY
)@@G@@                                          MCGS0880    @I@@@@  530 WTP(2)LZ
)@@G@@= WEIGHT                                                    MCGS0890    MA
)@@G@@@I@@@@      DO 641 J3= 1, L3                                            MB
)@@G@@      MCGS0900    @I@@@@      C(3)= A(3) + (2*J3-1)*H(3)                MC
)@@G@@                        MCGS0910    @I@@@@      DO 640 I3= M31, M32     MD
)@@G@@                                          MCGS0920    @I@@@@      X(3)= ME
)@@G@@C(3) + H(3)*V(I3)                                           MCGS0930    MF
)@@G@@@I@@@@      WEIGHT= WTP(2)*W(I3)                                        MG
)@@G@@      MCGS0940    @I@@@@      GO TO LAB3                                MH
)@@G@@                        MCGS0950    @I@@@@  531 SUM= SUM + WEIGHT*FUNEX(MI
)@@G@@X)                                        MCGS0960    @I@@@@      GO TO MJ
)@@G@@640                                                         MCGS0970    MK

)@@G@@SUBROUTINE NIMRGS (N, FA, FB, FUNEX, IP, NP, IS, NS, IOPT, VINT,$)M12300VQ
)@@G@@10    @I@@@@      DOUBLE PRECISION A, B, C, D, F, R, V, W               VR
)@@G@@            M1230020    @I@@@@      INTEGER OFFSET, P, S, H, BASE       VS
)@@G@@                              M1230030    @I@@@@      COMMON /QUAD20/ V(VT
)@@G@@210), W(210)                                    M1230040    @I@@@@      VU
)@@G@@EXTERNAL FA, FB, FUNEX                                            M12300VV
)@@G@@50    @I@@@@      DIMENSION A(6), B(6), C(6), D(7), R(7), X(6), IP(6), IVW
)@@G@@S(6),       M1230060    @I@@@@     * S(6), P(6), OFFSET(6), H(6), K(6), VX
)@@G@@XN(6), BASE(20)               M1230070    @I@@@@C     ******************VY
)@@G@@************************************************M1230080    @I@@@@C     VZ
)@@G@@NUMERICAL INTEGRATION OVER GENERAL REGIONS OF UP TO 6 DIMENSIONS. M12300WA
)@@G@@90    @I@@@@C     IN TERMS  OF FORTRAN FUNCTIONS, THE PROBLEM SOLVED IS WB
)@@G@@            M1230100    @I@@@@C                                         WC
)@@G@@                              M1230110    @I@@@@C        ***  FB(1,X)   WD
)@@G@@     ***  FB(2,X)            ***  FB(N,X)       M1230120    @I@@@@C     WE
)@@G@@   *                   *                       *                  M12301WF
)@@G@@30    @I@@@@C        *                   *                       *      WG
)@@G@@            M1230140    @I@@@@C        *  FUNEX(1,X) DX1   *  FUNEX(2,X)WH
)@@G@@ DX2 . . . *  FUNEX(N,X) DXN  M1230150    @I@@@@C        *              WI
)@@G@@     *                       *                  M1230160    @I@@@@C     WJ
)@@G@@   *                   *                       *                  M12301WK
)@@G@@70    @I@@@@C      ***  FA(1,X)        ***  FA(2,X)            ***  FA(NWL
)@@G@@,X)         M1230180    @I@@@@C                                         WM
)@@G@@                              M1230190    @I@@@@C     GAUSSIAN QUADRATURWN
)@@G@@E, WHOSE ORDER IS DETERMINED BY THE IP ARRAY    M1230200    @I@@@@C     WO
)@@G@@OR NP, (UP TO ORDER 20) IS USED OVER SUBREGIONS DETERMINED BY IS  M12302WP
)@@G@@10    @I@@@@C     ARRAY OR NS.  THIS CODE IS A MODIFICATION OF XINT / DXWQ
)@@G@@INT FROM    M1230220    @I@@@@C     THE UNIVERSITY OF MINNESOTA.        WR
)@@G@@                              M1230230    @I@@@@C     ******************WS
)@@G@@************************************************M1230240    @I@@@@C     WT
)@@G@@N      = DIMENSIONALITY                                           M12302WU
)@@G@@50    @I@@@@C     FA     = FUNCTION SPECIFYING LOWER LIMITS OF INTEGRATIWV
)@@G@@ON          M1230260    @I@@@@C     FB     = FUNCTION SPECIFYING UPPER LWW
)@@G@@IMITS OF INTEGRATION          M1230270    @I@@@@C     FUNEX  = FUNCTION WX
)@@G@@TO BE INTEGRATED                                M1230280    @I@@@@C     WY
)@@G@@IP     = ARRAY OF QUADRATURE ORDERS USED FOR EACH INTERVAL IF NP=0M12302WZ
)@@G@@90    @I@@@@C     NP     = QUADRATURE ORDER USED FOR EVERY INTERVAL IF PXA
)@@G@@OSITIVE     M1230300    @I@@@@C     IS     = ARRAY OF NO. SUBDIVISIONS UXB
)@@G@@SED FOR EACH INTERVAL IF NS=0 M1230310    @I@@@@C     NS     = NO. SUBDIXC
)@@G@@VISIONS USED FOR EVERY INTERVAL IF POSITIVE     M1230320    @I@@@@C     XD
)@@G@@IOPT   = OUTPUT OPTION                                            M12303XE
)@@G@@30    @I@@@@C     VINT   = COMPUTED ESTIMATE OF INTEGRAL                XF
)@@G@@            M1230340    @I@@@@C     $K     = RETURN TO STATEMENT K IF ERXG
)@@G@@RORS OCCUR                    M1230350    @I@@@@C     ******************XH
)@@G@@************************************************M1230360    @I@@@@      XI
)@@G@@DATA NCALL /0/                                                    M12303XJ
)@@G@@70    @I@@@@      DATA XN /.500000, .250000, .125000, .062500, .031250, XK
)@@G@@.015625/    M1230380    @I@@@@      DATA BASE /  0,   1,   3,   6,  10, XL
)@@G@@ 15,  21,  28,  36,  45,      M1230390    @I@@@@     *            55,  6XM
)@@G@@6,  78,  91, 105, 120, 136, 153, 171, 190/      M1230400    @I@@@@      XN
)@@G@@T0= TIMEF (0.)                                                    M12304XO
)@@G@@10    @I@@@@      NCALL= NCALL + 1                                      XP
)@@G@@            M1230420    @I@@@@      CALL NIGQ20                         XQ
)@@G@@                              M1230430    @I@[@@      NQUAD= 0          XR
)@@G@@                                                M1230435    @I@@@[      XS
)@@G@@NFEI= 0                                                           M12304XT
)@@G@@35    @I@@@[      NFEL= 0                                               XU
)@@G@@            M1230438    @I@@@@C     CHECK NO. PARAMETERS                XV
)@@G@@                              M1230440    @I@@@@      CALL URXITP(11)   XW
)@@G@@                                                M1230445    @I@@@@C     XX
)@@G@@CHECK FOR WARNINGS AND ERRORS                                     M12304XY
)@@G@@50    @I@@@@      IERR= -1                                              XZ
)@@G@@            M1230455    @I@@@@C     CHECK IF FA, FB, FUNEX ARE FUNCTIONSYA
)@@G@@                              M1230460    @I@@@@      INCODE= FLD (0, 6,YB
)@@G@@ FA)                                            M1230465    @I@@@@      YC
)@@G@@IF (INCODE .NE. 0 .AND. INCODE .NE. 63) GO TO 90                  M12304YD
)@@G@@70    @I@@@@      FNAME= 'F'                                            YE
)@@G@@            M1230475    @I@@@@      PRINT 105, FNAME                    YF
)@@G@@                              M1230480    @I@@@@      IERR= 1           YG
)@@G@@                                                M1230490    @I@@@@   90 YH
)@@G@@INCODE= FLD (0, 6, FB)                                            M12304YI
)@@G@@95    @I@@@@      IF (INCODE .NE. 0 .AND. INCODE .NE. 63) GO TO 100     YJ
)@@G@@            M1230500    @I@@@@      FNAME= 'G'                          YK
)@@G@@                              M1230505    @I@@@@      PRINT 105, FNAME  YL
)@@G@@                                                M1230510    @I@@@@      YM
)@@G@@IERR= 1                                                           M12305YN
)@@G@@15    @I@@@@  100 INCODE= FLD (0, 6, FUNEX)                             YO
)@@G@@            M1230520    @I@@@@      IF (INCODE .NE. 0 .AND. INCODE .NE. YP
)@@G@@63) GO TO 110                 M1230525    @I@@@@      FNAME= 'U'        YQ
)@@G@@                                                M1230530    @I@@@@      YR
)@@G@@PRINT 105, FNAME                                                  M12305YS
)@@G@@35    @I@@@@  105 FORMAT (1H0,'*ERROR, ',A1,' IS NOT THE NAME OF A FUNCTYT
)@@G@@ION ',      M1230540    @I@@@@     * 'SUBPROGRAM.')                     YU
)@@G@@                              M1230545    @I@@@@      IERR= 1           YV
)@@G@@                                                M1230550    @I@@@@C     YW
)@@G@@CHECK N, NP, NS                                                   M12305YX
)@@G@@55    @I@@@@  110 IF (N .GE. 1 .AND. N .LE. 6) GO TO 120                YY
)@@G@@            M1230560    @I@@@@      PRINT 115, N                        YZ
)@@G@@                              M1230565    @I@@@@  115 FORMAT (1H0,'*ERROZA
)@@G@@R, N =',I12,',  N MUST BE .GE. 1 AND .LE. 6.')  M1230570    @I@@@@      ZB
)@@G@@IERR= 1                                                           M12305ZC
)@@G@@75    @I@@@@  120 IF (NP .GE. 0 .AND. NP .LE. 20) GO TO 130             ZD
)@@G@@            M1230580    @I@@@@      PRINT 125, NP                       ZE
)@@G@@                              M1230585    @I@@@@  125 FORMAT(1H0,'*ERRORZF
)@@G@@, NP =',I12,',  NP MUST BE .GE. 0 AND .LE. 20.')M1230590    @I@@@@      ZG
)@@G@@IERR= 1                                                           M12305ZH
)@@G@@95    @I@@@@  130 IF (NS .GE. 0) GO TO 140                              ZI
)@@G@@            M1230600    @I@@@@      PRINT 135, NS                       ZJ
)@@G@@                              M1230605    @I@@@@  135 FORMAT (1H0,'*ERROZK
)@@G@@R, NS =',I12,',  NS MUST BE .GE. 0.')           M1230610    @I@@@@      ZL
)@@G@@IERR= 1                                                           M12306ZM
)@@G@@15    @I@@@@C     CHECK IOPT (WARNING ONLY)                             ZN
)@@G@@            M1230620    @I@@@@  140 IF (IOPT .EQ. 0 .OR. IOPT .EQ. 1) GOZO
)@@G@@ TO 150                       M1230625    @I@@@@      PRINT 145, IOPT   ZP
)@@G@@                                                M1230630    @I@@@@  145 ZQ
)@@G@@FORMAT (1H0,'*WARNING, IOPT IS NOT 0 OR 1, IOPT =', I12,          M12306ZR
)@@G@@35    @I@@@@     * ',  IOPT = 1 ASSUMED.')                              ZS
)@@G@@            M1230640    @I@@@@      IERR= MAX(0,IERR)                   ZT
)@@G@@                              M1230645    @I@@@@C     TERMINTAE IF ERRORZU
)@@G@@S OCCURED                                       M1230650    @I@@@@  150 ZV
)@@G@@IF (IERR) 200, 153, 1000                                          M12306ZW
)@@G@@55    @I@@@@  153 PRINT 155                                             ZX
)@@G@@            M1230660    @I@@@@  155 FORMAT (1H0)                        ZY
)@@G@@                              M1230665    @I@@@@      CALL URWALK ('NIMRZZ
)@@G@@GS', 0)                                         M1230670    @I@@@@C     AA
)@@G@@INITIALIZATIONS                                                   M12306AB
)@@G@@80    @I@@@@  200 IF (NP) 210, 210, 250                                 AC
)@@G@@            M1230690    @I@@@@  210 DO 230 J= 1, N                      AD
)@@G@@                              M1230700    @I@@@@      L= IP(J)          AE
)@@G@@                                                M1230710    @I@@@@C     AF
)@@G@@ERROR IF NOT 1 TO 20                                              M12307AG
)@@G@@20    @I@@@@      IF (L .LT. 1 .OR. L .GT. 20) GO TO 240                AH
)@@G@@            M1230730    @I@@@@      OFFSET(J)= BASE(L)                  AI
)@@G@@                              M1230740    @I@@@@  230 P(J)= L           AJ
)@@G@@                                                M1230750    @I@@@@      AK
)@@G@@GO TO 300                                                         M12307AL
)@@G@@60    @I@@@@  240 PRINT 245, (IP(J), J= 1, N)                           AM
)@@G@@            M1230770    @I@@@@  245 FORMAT (1H0, '*ERROR, NP = 0 AND SOMAN
)@@G@@E IP(J) .LT. 1 OR .GT. 20.'/  M1230780    @I@@@@     * 1H0, 8X, 'IP CONTAO
)@@G@@AINS ', 6I13)                                   M1230790    @I@@@@      AP
)@@G@@IERR= 1                                                           M12308AQ
)@@G@@00    @I@@@@      GO TO 300                                             AR
)@@G@@            M1230810    @I@@@@  250 DO 260 J= 1, N                      AS
)@@G@@                              M1230820    @I@@@@      OFFSET(J)= BASE(NPAT
)@@G@@)                                               M1230830    @I@@@@  260 AU
)@@G@@P(J)= NP                                                          M12308AV
)@@G@@40    @I@@@@  300 IF (NS) 310, 310, 350                                 AW
)@@G@@            M1230850    @I@@@@  310 DO 330 J= 1, N                      AX
)@@G@@                              M1230860    @I@@@@C     ERROR IF NOT POSITAY
)@@G@@IVE                                             M1230870    @I@@@@      AZ
)@@G@@IF (IS(J)) 340, 340, 330                                          M12308BA
)@@G@@80    @I@@@@  330 S(J)= IS(J)                                           BB
)@@G@@            M1230890    @I@@@@      GO TO 400                           BC
)@@G@@                              M1230900    @I@@@@  340 PRINT 345, (IS(J),BD
)@@G@@ J= 1, N)                                       M1230920    @I@@@@  345 BE
)@@G@@FORMAT (1H0,'*ERROR, NS = 0 AND SOME IS(J) .LT. 1.'/              M12309BF
)@@G@@30    @I@@@@     * 1H0, 8X, 'IS CONTAINS ', 6I13)                       BG
)@@G@@            M1230940    @I@@@@      IERR= 1                             BH
)@@G@@                              M1230950    @I@@@@      GO TO 400         BI
)@@G@@                                                M1230960    @I@@@@  350 BJ
)@@G@@DO 360 J= 1, N                                                    M12309BK
)@@G@@70    @I@@@@  360 S(J)= NS                                              BL
)@@G@@            M1230980    @I@@@@C     TERMINATE IF ERRORS OCCURED         BM
)@@G@@                              M1230990    @I@]@@  400 IF (IERR) 430, 430BN
)@@G@@, 1000                                          M1231000    @I@@[]  400 BO
)@@G@@IF (IERR) 410, 410, 1000                                          M12310BP
)@@G@@00    @I[@@[C     COMPUTE NO. QUADRATURE POINTS                         BQ
)@@G@@            M1231002    @I@]@[      NQUAD= 1                            BR
)@@G@@                              M1231004    @I@@[]  410 NQUAD= 1          BS
)@@G@@                                                M1231004    @I[@@[      BT
)@@G@@DO 420 J= 1, N                                                    M12310BU
)@@G@@06    @I@@@[  420 NQUAD= NQUAD*P(J)*S(J)                                BV
)@@G@@            M1231008    @I@@@@C     ************************************BW
)@@G@@******************************M1231010    @I@@@@C     INTEGRATION       BX
)@@G@@                                                M1231020    @I@@@@  430 BY
)@@G@@DO 456 J= 1, N                                                    M12310BZ
)@@G@@30    @I@@@@  456 X(J)= 0.                                              CA
)@@G@@            M1231040    @I@@@@      M= 1                                CB
)@@G@@                              M1231060    @I@@@@      R(N+1)= 1.        CC
)@@G@@                                                M1231070    @I@@@@      CD
)@@G@@D(N+1)= 1.                                                        M12310CE
)@@G@@80    @I@@@@  501 DO 540 J= M, N                                        CF
)@@G@@            M1231090    @I@@@@      A(J)= FA(J,X)                       CG
)@@G@@                              M1231100    @I@@@@      B(J)= FB(J,X)     CH
)@@G@@                                                M1231110    @I@@@[      CI
)@@G@@NFEL= NFEL + 2                                                    M12311CJ
)@@G@@15    @I@@@@      D(J)= (B(J) - A(J)) / FLOAT(S(J))                     CK
)@@G@@            M1231120    @I@@@@      C(J)= A(J) + 0.5*D(J)               CL
)@@G@@                              M1231130    @I@@@@      IV= OFFSET(J) + 1 CM
)@@G@@                                                M1231140    @I@@@@      CN
)@@G@@X(J)= C(J) + 0.5*D(J)*V(IV)                                       M12311CO
)@@G@@50    @I@@@@      R(J)= 0.                                              CP
)@@G@@            M1231160    @I@@@@      H(J)= 1                             CQ
)@@G@@                              M1231170    @I@@@@  540 K(J)= 1           CR
)@@G@@                                                M1231180    @I@@@@      CS
)@@G@@J= N                                                              M12311CT
)@@G@@90    @I@@@@  631 IW= K(J) + OFFSET(J)                                  CU
)@@G@@            M1231200    @I@@@@      F= FUNEX(J,X)                       CV
)@@G@@                              M1231210    @I@[@@      NQUAD= NQUAD + 1  CW
)@@G@@                                                M1231215    @I@@@[      CX
)@@G@@NFEI= NFEI + 1                                                    M12312CY
)@@G@@15    @I@@@@      R(J)= R(J) + R(J+1)*D(J+1)*F*W(IW)                    CZ
)@@G@@            M1231220    @I@@@@      IF (K(J) .GE. P(J)) GO TO 756       DA
)@@G@@                              M1231230    @I@@@@      K(J)= K(J) + 1    DB
)@@G@@                                                M1231240    @I@@@@  701 DC

)@@G@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@*[S@@@*SDFF*@I@@[@      SUBROUTINE NIX3PT (A, B,BY
)@@G@@ RESULT, K, EPSIL, NPTS, ICHECK, F)       QUAD0010    @I[@@@      DOUBLEBZ
)@@G@@ PRECISION P                                                            CA
)@@G@@@I@@@@      DIMENSION FUNCT(127), P(381), RESULT(8)                     CB
)@@G@@      QUAD  20    @I@@@@C THIS SUBROUTINE ATTEMPTS TO CALCULATE THE INTECC
)@@G@@GRAL OF F(X)            QUAD  30    @I@@@@C OVER THE INTERVAL *A* TO *B*CD
)@@G@@ WITH RELATIVE ERROR NOT                  QUAD  40    @I@@@@C EXCEEDING CE
)@@G@@*EPSIL*.                                                    QUAD  50    CF
)@@G@@@I@@@@C THE RESULT IS OBTAINED USING A SEQUENCE OF 1,3,7,15,31,63,      CG
)@@G@@      QUAD  60    @I@@@@C 127, AND 255 POINT INTERLACING FORMULAE(NO INTCH
)@@G@@EGRAND                  QUAD  70    @I@@@@C EVALUATIONS ARE WASTED) OF RCI
)@@G@@ESPECTIVE DEGREE 1,5,11,23,               QUAD  80    @I@@@@C 47,95,191 CJ
)@@G@@AND 383. THE FORMULAE ARE BASED ON THE OPTIMAL              QUAD  90    CK
)@@G@@@I@@@@C EXTENSION OF THE 3-POINT GAUSS FORMULA.  DETAILS OF             CL
)@@G@@      QUAD 100    @I@@@@C THE FORMULAE ARE GIVEN IN *THE OPTIMUM ADDITIOCM
)@@G@@N OF POINTS             QUAD 110    @I@@@@C TO QUADRATURE FORMULAE* BY TCN
)@@G@@.N.L. PATTERSON,MATHS.COMP.               QUAD 120    @I@@@@C VOL 22,847CO
)@@G@@-856,1968.                                                  QUAD 130    CP
)@@G@@@I@@@@C                     *** INPUT ***                               CQ
)@@G@@      QUAD 140    @I@@@@C A       LOWER LIMIT OF INTEGRATION.           CR
)@@G@@                        QUAD 150    @I@@@@C B       UPPER LIMIT OF INTEGCS
)@@G@@RATION.                                   QUAD 160    @I@@@@C EPSIL   RECT
)@@G@@LATIVE ACCURACY REQUIRED. WHEN THE RELATIVE                 QUAD 170    CU
)@@G@@@I@@@@C         DIFFERENCE OF TWO SUCCESSIVE FORMULAE DOES NOT          CV
)@@G@@      QUAD 180    @I@@@@C         EXCEED *EPSIL* THE LAST FORMULA COMPUTCW
)@@G@@ED IS TAKEN             QUAD 190    @I@@@@C         AS THE RESULT.      CX
)@@G@@                                          QUAD 200    @I@@@@C F       F(CY
)@@G@@X) IS THE INTEGRAND.                                        QUAD 210    CZ
)@@G@@@I@@@@C                     *** OUTPUT ***                              DA
)@@G@@      QUAD 220    @I@@@@C RESULT  THIS ARRAY,WHICH SHOULD BE DECLARED TODB
)@@G@@ HAVE AT                QUAD 230    @I@@@@C         LEAST 8 ELEMENTS, HODC
)@@G@@LDS THE RESULTS OBTAINED BY               QUAD 240    @I@@@@C         THDD
)@@G@@E 1,3,7, ETC., POINT FORMULAE. THE NUMBER OF                QUAD 250    DE
)@@G@@@I@@@@C         FORMULAE COMPUTED DEPENTS ON *EPSIL*.                   DF
)@@G@@      QUAD 260    @I@@@@C K       RESULT(K) HOLDS THE VALUE OF THE INTEGDG
)@@G@@RAL TO THE              QUAD 270    @I@@@@C         SPECIFIED RELATIVE ADH
)@@G@@CCURACY.                                  QUAD 280    @I@@@@C NPTS    NUDI
)@@G@@MBER INTEGRAND EVALUATIONS.                                 QUAD 290    DJ
)@@G@@@I@@@@C ICHECK  ON EXIT NORMALLY ICHECK=0. HOWEVER IF CONVERGENCE       DK
)@@G@@      QUAD 300    @I@@@@C         TO THE ACCURACY REQUESTED IS NOT ACHIEDL
)@@G@@VED ICHECK=1            QUAD 310    @I@@@@C         ON EXIT.            DM
)@@G@@                                          QUAD 320    @I@@@@C ABSCISSAE DN
)@@G@@AND WEIGHTS OF QUADRATURE RULES ARE STACKED IN              QUAD 330    DO
)@@G@@@I@@@@C ARRAY *P* IN THE ORDER IN WHICH THEY ARE NEEDED.                DP
)@@G@@      QUAD 340    @I@@@@      DATA                                      DQ
)@@G@@                        QUAD 350    @I@@@@     * P( 1),P( 2),P( 3),P( 4)DR
)@@G@@,P( 5),P( 6),P( 7),                       QUAD 360    @I@@@@     * P( 8)DS
)@@G@@,P( 9),P(10),P(11),P(12),P(13),P(14),                       QUAD 370    DT
)@@G@@@I@@@@     * P(15),P(16),P(17),P(18),P(19),P(20),P(21),                 DU
)@@G@@      QUAD 380    @I@@@@     * P(22),P(23),P(24),P(25),P(26),P(27),P(28)DV
)@@G@@/                       QUAD 390    @I@@@@     *  0.774596669241483377  DW

)@@G@@@I@@@@      FZERO = F(SUM)                                              QM

)@@G@@ 0                                                          QUAD3050    QQ

)@@G@@                        QUAD3070    @I@@@@      ACUM = 0.0              QT
)@@G@@                                          QUAD3080    @I@@@@      GO TO QU

)@@G@@                        QUAD3110    @I@@@@      ACUM = 0.0              QY
)@@G@@                                          QUAD3120    @I@@@@C CONTRIBUTIQZ

)@@G@@CT(J)                                     QUAD3160    @I@@@@   20 CONTINRE
)@@G@@UE                                                          QUAD3170    RF

)@@G@@                                          QUAD3200    @I@@@@        I = RJ

)@@G@@                        QUAD3230    @I@@@@        I = I + 1             RN
)@@G@@                                          QUAD3240    @I@@@@        ACUMRO
)@@G@@ = ACUM + P(I)*FUNCT(J)                                     QUAD3250    RP
)@@G@@@I@@@@   40 CONTINUE                                                    RQ

)@@G@@                        QUAD3270    @I@@@@      I = I + 1               RS

)@@G@@ESULT(K))) 60,          QUAD3310    @I@@@@     * 60, 10                 RX

)@@G@@@@^@@]@@A@@[@@C@@[@@G@@@@@]@IS@C@@]7NERR3$      NIX3PT      @@[@@@@@@@]OWP
)@@G@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@WQ
)@@G@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@*[S@@@*SDFF*@I@@@@      SUBROUTINE NIXSLA (A, B,WR
)@@G@@ EPSIL, NPTS, ICHECK, RELERR, F, QSUBA)   QSBA0010    @I@@@@C   THIS FUNWS
)@@G@@CTION ROUTINE PERFORMS AUTOMATIC INTEGRATION                QSBA  20    WT
)@@G@@@I@@@@C OVER A FINITE INTERVAL USING THE BASIC INTEGRATION              WU
)@@G@@      QSBA  30    @I@@@@C ALGORITHM QUAD TOGETHER WITH,  IF NECESSARY ANWV
)@@G@@ ADAPTIVE               QSBA  40    @I@@@@C SUBDIVISION PROCESS.  IT IS WW
)@@G@@GENERALLY MORE EFFICIENT THAN             QSBA  50    @I@@@@C THE NON-ADWX
)@@G@@APTIVE ALGORITHM QSUB BUT IS LIKELY TO BE LESS              QSBA  60    WY
)@@G@@@I@@@@C RELIABLE(SEE COMP.J.,14,189,1971).                              WZ
)@@G@@      QSBA  70    @I@@@@C   THE CALL TAKES THE FORM                     XA
)@@G@@                        QSBA  80    @I@@@@C           QSUBA(A,B,EPSIL,NPXB
)@@G@@TS,ICHECK,RELERR,F)                       QSBA  90    @I@@@@C AND CAUSESXC
)@@G@@ F(X) TO BE INTEGRATED OVER (A,B) WITH RELATIVE             QSBA 100    XD
)@@G@@@I@@@@C ERROR HOPEFULLY NOT EXCEEDING EPSIL.  SHOULD QUAD CONVERGE      XE
)@@G@@      QSBA 110    @I@@@@C (ICHECK=0) THEN QSUBA WILL RETURN THE VALUE OBXF
)@@G@@TAINED BY IT            QSBA 120    @I@@@@C OTHERWISE SUBDIVISION WILL BXG
)@@G@@E INVOKED AS A RESCUE                     QSBA 130    @I@@@@C OPERATION XH
)@@G@@IN AN ADAPTIVE MANNER. THE ARGUMENT RELERR GIVES            QSBA 140    XI
)@@G@@@I@@@@C A CRUDE ESTIMATE OF THE ACTUAL RELATIVE ERROR OBTAINED.         XJ
)@@G@@      QSBA 150    @I@@@@C   THE SUBDIVISION STRATEGY IS AS FOLLOWS      XK
)@@G@@                        QSBA 160    @I@@@@C AT EACH STAGE OF THE PROCESSXL
)@@G@@ AN INTERVAL IS PRESENTED FOR             QSBA 170    @I@@@@C SUBDIVISIOXM
)@@G@@N (INITIALLY THIS WILL BE THE WHOLE INTERVAL                QSBA 180    XN
)@@G@@@I@@@@C (A,B)).  THE INTERVAL IS HALVED AND QUAD APPLIED TO EACH        XO
)@@G@@      QSBA 190    @I@@@@C SUBINTERVAL.  SHOULD QUAD FAIL ON THE FIRST SUXP
)@@G@@BINTERVAL               QSBA 200    @I@@@@C THE SUBINTERVAL IS STACKED FXQ
)@@G@@OR FUTURE SUBDIVISION AND THE             QSBA 210    @I@@@@C SECOND SUBXR
)@@G@@INTERVAL IMMEDIATELY EXAMINED.  SHOULD QUAD FAIL            QSBA 220    XS
)@@G@@@I@@@@C ON THE SECOND SUBINTERVAL THE SUBINTERVAL IS                    XT
)@@G@@      QSBA 230    @I@@@@C IMMEDIATELY SUBDIVIDED AND THE WHOLE PROCESS RXU
)@@G@@EPEATED.                QSBA 240    @I@@@@C EACH TIME A CONVERGED RESULTXV
)@@G@@ IS OBTAINED IT IS                        QSBA 250    @I@@@@C ACCUMULATEXW
)@@G@@D AS THE PARTIAL VALUE OF THE INTEGRAL. WHEN                QSBA 260    XX
)@@G@@@I@@@@C QUAD CONVERGES ON BOTH SUBINTERVALS THE INTERVAL LAST           XY
)@@G@@      QSBA 270    @I@@@@C STACKED IS CHOSEN NEXT FOR SUBDIVISION AND THEXZ
)@@G@@ PROCESS                QSBA 280    @I@@@@C REPEATED.  A SUBINTERVAL IS YA
)@@G@@NOT EXAMINED AGAIN ONCE A                 QSBA 290    @I@@@@C CONVERGED YB
)@@G@@RESULT IS OBTAINED FOR IT SO THAT A SPURIOUS                QSBA 300    YC
)@@G@@@I@@@@C CONVERGENCE IS MORE LIKELY TO SLIP THROUGH THAN FOR THE         YD
)@@G@@      QSBA 310    @I@@@@C NON-ADAPTIVE ALGORITHM QSUB.                  YE
)@@G@@                        QSBA 320    @I@@@@C   THE CONVERGENCE CRITERION YF
)@@G@@OF QUAD IS SLIGHTLY RELAXED               QSBA 330    @I@@@@C IN THAT A YG
)@@G@@PANEL IS DEEMED TO HAVE BEEN SUCCESSFULLY                   QSBA 340    YH
)@@G@@@I@@@@C INTEGRATED IF EITHER QUAD CONVERGES OR THE ESTIMATED            YI
)@@G@@      QSBA 350    @I@@@@C ABSOLUTE ERROR COMMITTED ON THIS PANEL DOES NOYJ
)@@G@@T EXCEED                QSBA 360    @I@@@@C EPSIL TIMES THE ESTIMATED ABYK
)@@G@@SOLUTE VALUE OF THE INTEGRAL              QSBA 370    @I@@@@C OVER (A,B)YL
)@@G@@.  THIS RELAXATION IS TO TRY TO TAKE ACCOUNT OF             QSBA 380    YM
)@@G@@@I@@@@C A COMMON SITUATION WHERE ONE PARTICULAR PANEL CAUSES            YN
)@@G@@      QSBA 390    @I@@@@C SPECIAL DIFFICULTY, PERHAPS DUE TO A SINGULARIYO
)@@G@@TY OF SOME              QSBA 400    @I@@@@C TYPE.  IN THIS CASE QUAD COUYP
)@@G@@LD OBTAIN NEARLY EXACT                    QSBA 410    @I@@@@C ANSWERS ONYQ
)@@G@@ ALL OTHER PANELS AND SO THE RELATIVE ERROR FOR             QSBA 420    YR
)@@G@@@I@@@@C THE TOTAL INTEGRATION WOULD BE ALMOST ENTIRELY DUE TO THE       YS
)@@G@@      QSBA 430    @I@@@@C DELINQUENT PANEL.  WITHOUT THIS CONDITION THE YT
)@@G@@COMPUTATION             QSBA 440    @I@@@@C MIGHT CONTINUE DESPITE THE RYU
)@@G@@EQUESTED RELATIVE ERROR BEING             QSBA 450    @I@@@@C ACHIEVED. YV
)@@G@@                                                            QSBA 460    YW
)@@G@@@I@@@@C   THE OUTCOME OF THE INTEGRATION IS INDICATED BY ICHECK.        YX
)@@G@@      QSBA 470    @I@@@@C   ICHECK=0  -  CONVERGENCE OBTAINED WITHOUT INYY
)@@G@@VOKING SUB-             QSBA 480    @I@@@@C                DIVISION.  THYZ
)@@G@@IS WOULD CORRESPOND TO THE                QSBA 490    @I@@@@C           ZA
)@@G@@     DIRECT USE OF QUAD.                                    QSBA 500    ZB
)@@G@@@I@@@@C   ICHECK=1  -  RESULT OBTAINED AFTER INVOKING SUBDIVISION.      ZC
)@@G@@      QSBA 510    @I@@@@C   ICHECK=2  -  AS FOR ICHECK=1 BUT AT SOME POIZD
)@@G@@NT THE                  QSBA 520    @I@@@@C                RELAXED CONVEZE
)@@G@@RGENCE CRITERION WAS USED.                QSBA 530    @I@@@@C           ZF
)@@G@@     THE RISK OF UNDERESTIMATING THE RELATIVE               QSBA 540    ZG
)@@G@@@I@@@@C                ERROR WILL BE INCREASED.  IF NECESSARY,          ZH
)@@G@@      QSBA 550    @I@@@@C                CONFIDENCE MAY BE RESTORED BY CZI
)@@G@@HECKING                 QSBA 560    @I@@@@C                EPSIL AND RELZJ
)@@G@@ERR FOR A SERIOUS DISCREPANCY.            QSBA 570    @I@@@@C   ICHECK NZK
)@@G@@EGATIVE                                                     QSBA 580    ZL
)@@G@@@I@@@@C                IF DURING THE SUBDIVISION PROCESS THE STACK      ZM
)@@G@@      QSBA 590    @I@@@@C                OF DELINQUENT INTERVALS BECOMESZN
)@@G@@ FULL (IT IS            QSBA 600    @I@@@@C                PRESENTLY SETZO
)@@G@@ TO HOLD AT MOST 100 NUMBERS)             QSBA 610    @I@@@@C           ZP
)@@G@@     A RESULT IS OBTAINED BY CONTINUING THE                 QSBA 620    ZQ
)@@G@@@I@@@@C                INTEGRATION IGNORING CONVERGENCE FAILURES        ZR
)@@G@@      QSBA 630    @I@@@@C                WHICH CANNOT BE ACCOMMODATED ONZS
)@@G@@ THE STACK.             QSBA 640    @I@@@@C                THIS OCCURRENZT
)@@G@@CE IS FLAGGED BY RETURNING                QSBA 650    @I@@@@C           ZU
)@@G@@     ICHECK WITH NEGATIVE SIGN.                             QSBA 660    ZV
)@@G@@@I@@@@C  THE RELIABILITY OF THE ALGORITHM WILL DECREASE FOR LARGE       ZW
)@@G@@      QSBA 670    @I@@@@C  VALUES OF EPSIL.  IT IS RECOMMENDED THAT EPSIZX
)@@G@@L SHOULD                QSBA 680    @I@@@@C  GENERALLY BE LESS THAN ABOUZY
)@@G@@T 0.001.                                  QSBA 690    @I@@@@      DIMENSZZ
)@@G@@ION RESULT(8), STACK(100)                                   QSBA 700    AA
)@@G@@@I@@@@      EXTERNAL F                                                  AB
)@@G@@      QSBA 710    @I@@@@      DATA ISMAX/100/                           AC
)@@G@@                        QSBA 720    @I@@@@      CALL NIX3PT (A, B, RESULAD
)@@G@@T, K, EPSIL, NPTS, ICHECK, F)             QSBA0730    @I@@@@      QSUBA AE
)@@G@@= RESULT(K)                                                 QSBA 740    AF
)@@G@@@I@@@@      RELERR = 0.0                                                AG
)@@G@@      QSBA 750    @I@@@@      IF (QSUBA.NE.0.0) RELERR =                AH
)@@G@@                        QSBA 760    @I@@@@     * ABS((RESULT(K)-RESULT(KAI
)@@G@@-1))/QSUBA)                               QSBA 770    @I@@@@C CHECK IF SAJ
)@@G@@UBDIVISION IS NEEDED                                        QSBA 780    AK
)@@G@@@I@@@@      IF (ICHECK.EQ.0) RETURN                                     AL
)@@G@@      QSBA 790    @I@@@@C SUBDIVIDE                                     AM
)@@G@@                        QSBA 800    @I@@@@      ESTIM = ABS(QSUBA*EPSIL)AN
)@@G@@                                          QSBA 810    @I@@@@      RELERRAO
)@@G@@ = 0.0                                                      QSBA 820    AP
)@@G@@@I@@@@      QSUBA = 0.0                                                 AQ
)@@G@@      QSBA 830    @I@@@@      IS = 1                                    AR
)@@G@@                        QSBA 840    @I@@@@      IC = 1                  AS
)@@G@@                                          QSBA 850    @I@@@@      SUB1 =AT
)@@G@@ A                                                          QSBA 860    AU
)@@G@@@I@@@@      SUB3 = B                                                    AV
)@@G@@      QSBA 870    @I@@@@   10 SUB2 = (SUB1+SUB3)*0.5                    AW
)@@G@@                        QSBA 880    @I@@[@      CALL NIX3PT (SUB1, SUB2,AX
)@@G@@ RESULT, K, EPSIL, NF, ICHECK, F)         QSBA0890    @I[@@@      NPTS =AY
)@@G@@ NPTS + NF                                                  QSBA 900    AZ
)@@G@@@I@@@@      COMP = ABS(RESULT(K)-RESULT(K-1))                           BA
)@@G@@      QSBA 910    @I@@@@      IF (ICHECK.EQ.0) GO TO 30                 BB
)@@G@@                        QSBA 920    @I@@@@      IF (COMP.LE.ESTIM) GO TOBC
)@@G@@ 70                                       QSBA 930    @I@@@@      IF (ISBD
)@@G@@.GE.ISMAX) GO TO 20                                         QSBA 940    BE
)@@G@@@I@@@@C STACK SUBINTERVAL (SUB1,SUB2) FOR FUTURE EXAMINATION            BF
)@@G@@      QSBA 950    @I@@@@      STACK(IS) = SUB1                          BG
)@@G@@                        QSBA 960    @I@@@@      IS = IS + 1             BH
)@@G@@                                          QSBA 970    @I@@@@      STACK(BI
)@@G@@IS) = SUB2                                                  QSBA 980    BJ
)@@G@@@I@@@@      IS = IS + 1                                                 BK
)@@G@@      QSBA 990    @I@@@@      GO TO 40                                  BL
)@@G@@                        QSBA1000    @I@@@@   20 IC = -IABS(IC)          BM
)@@G@@                                          QSBA1010    @I@@@@   30 QSUBA BN
)@@G@@= QSUBA + RESULT(K)                                         QSBA1020    BO
)@@G@@@I@@@@      RELERR = RELERR + COMP                                      BP
)@@G@@      QSBA1030    @I@@[@   40 CALL NIX3PT (SUB2, SUB3, RESULT, K, EPSIL,BQ
)@@G@@ NF, ICHECK, F)         QSBA1040    @I[@@@      NPTS = NPTS + NF        BR
)@@G@@                                          QSBA1050    @I@@@@      COMP =BS
)@@G@@ ABS(RESULT(K)-RESULT(K-1))                                 QSBA1060    BT
)@@G@@@I@@@@      IF (ICHECK.EQ.0) GO TO 50                                   BU
)@@G@@      QSBA1070    @I@@@@      IF (COMP.LE.ESTIM) GO TO 80               BV
)@@G@@                        QSBA1080    @I@@@@C SUBDIVIDE INTERVAL (SUB2,SUBBW
)@@G@@3)                                        QSBA1090    @I@@@@      SUB1 =BX
)@@G@@ SUB2                                                       QSBA1100    BY
)@@G@@@I@@@@      GO TO 10                                                    BZ
)@@G@@      QSBA1110    @I@@@@   50 QSUBA = QSUBA + RESULT(K)                 CA
)@@G@@                        QSBA1120    @I@@@@      RELERR = RELERR + COMP  CB
)@@G@@                                          QSBA1130    @I@@@@      IF (ISCC
)@@G@@.EQ.1) GO TO 60                                             QSBA1140    CD
)@@G@@@I@@@@C SUBDIVIDE THE DELINQUENT INTERVAL LAST STACKED                  CE
)@@G@@      QSBA1150    @I@@@@      IS = IS - 1                               CF
)@@G@@                        QSBA1160    @I@@@@      SUB3 = STACK(IS)        CG
)@@G@@                                          QSBA1170    @I@@@@      IS = ICH
)@@G@@S - 1                                                       QSBA1180    CI
)@@G@@@I@@@@      SUB1 = STACK(IS)                                            CJ
)@@G@@      QSBA1190    @I@@@@      GO TO 10                                  CK
)@@G@@                        QSBA1200    @I@@@@C SUBDIVISION RESULT          CL
)@@G@@                                          QSBA1210    @I@@@@   60 ICHECKCM
)@@G@@ = IC                                                       QSBA1220    CN
)@@G@@@I@@@@      RELERR = RELERR/ABS(QSUBA)                                  CO
)@@G@@      QSBA1230    @I@@@@      RETURN                                    CP
)@@G@@                        QSBA1240    @I@@@@C RELAXED CONVERGENCE         CQ
)@@G@@                                          QSBA1250    @I@@@@   70 IC = ICR
)@@G@@SIGN(2,IC)                                                  QSBA1260    CS
)@@G@@@I@@@@      GO TO 30                                                    CT
)@@G@@      QSBA1270    @I@@@@   80 IC = ISIGN(2,IC)                          CU
)@@G@@                        QSBA1280    @I@@@@      GO TO 50                CV
)@@G@@                                          QSBA1290    @I@@@@      END   CW
)@@G@@                                                            QSBA1300    CX

)@@G@@@@[@@@@@@@],B@@@@W^)3N>"10173+VFCBED0945@YB@@@@W^)3N>"10173+VFCBED0946@YEE
)@@G@@B@@@@4^)3N>"10173+VFCBED*[S@@@*SDFF*@I@@@@      SUBROUTINE NIXSLB (A, B,EF
)@@G@@ EPSIL, NPTS, ICHECK, RELERR, F, QSUB)    QSUB0010    @I@@@@C   THIS FUNEG
)@@G@@CTION ROUTINE PERFORMS AUTOMATIC INTEGRATION                QSUB  20    EH
)@@G@@@I@@@@C OVER A FINITE INTERVAL USING THE BASIC INTEGRATION              EI
)@@G@@      QSUB  30    @I@@@@C ALGORITHM QUAD, TOGETHER WITH, IF NECESSARY, AEJ
)@@G@@ NON-                   QSUB  40    @I@@@@C ADAPTIVE SUBDIVISION PROCESSEK
)@@G@@.                                         QSUB  50    @I@@@@C   THE CALLEL
)@@G@@ TAKES THE FORM                                             QSUB  60    EM
)@@G@@@I@@@@C            QSUB(A,B,EPSIL,NPTS,ICHECK,RELERR,F)                 EN
)@@G@@      QSUB  70    @I@@@@C AND CAUSES F(X) TO BE INTEGRATED OVER (A,B) WIEO
)@@G@@TH RELATIVE             QSUB  80    @I@@@@C ERROR HOPEFULLY NOT EXCEEDINEP
)@@G@@G EPSIL.  SHOULD QUAD CONVERGE            QSUB  90    @I@@@@C (ICHECK=0)EQ
)@@G@@ THEN QSUB WILL RETURN THE VALUE OBTAINED BY IT             QSUB 100    ER
)@@G@@@I@@@@C OTHERWISE SUBDIVISION WILL BE INVOKED AS A RESCUE               ES
)@@G@@      QSUB 110    @I@@@@C OPERATION IN A NON-ADAPTIVE MANNER. THE ARGUMEET
)@@G@@NT RELERR               QSUB 120    @I@@@@C GIVES A CRUDE ESTIMATE OF THEU
)@@G@@E ACTUAL RELATIVE ERROR                   QSUB 130    @I@@@@C OBTAINED. EV
)@@G@@                                                            QSUB 140    EW
)@@G@@@I@@@@C   THE SUBDIVISION STRATEGY IS AS FOLLOWS                        EX
)@@G@@      QSUB 150    @I@@@@C LET THE INTERVAL (A,B) BE DIVIDED INTO 2**N PAEY
)@@G@@NELS AT STEP            QSUB 160    @I@@@@C N OF THE SUBDIVISION PROCESSEZ
)@@G@@.  QUAD IS APPLIED FIRST TO               QSUB 170    @I@@@@C THE SUBDIVFA
)@@G@@IDED INTERVAL ON WHICH QUAD LAST FAILED TO                  QSUB 180    FB
)@@G@@@I@@@@C CONVERGE AND IF CONVERGENCE IS NOW ACHIEVED THE REMAINING       FC
)@@G@@      QSUB 190    @I@@@@C PANELS ARE INTEGRATED. SHOULD A CONVERGENCE FAFD
)@@G@@ILURE OCCUR             QSUB 200    @I@@@@C ON ANY PANEL THE INTEGRATIONFE
)@@G@@ AT THAT POINT IS TERMINATED              QSUB 210    @I@@@@C AND THE PRFF
)@@G@@OCEDURE REPEATED WITH N INCREASED BY 1. THE                 QSUB 220    FG
)@@G@@@I@@@@C STRATEGY INSURES THAT POSSIBLY DELINQUENT INTERVALS ARE         FH
)@@G@@      QSUB 230    @I@@@@C EXAMINED BEFORE WORK, WHICH LATER MIGHT HAVE TFI
)@@G@@O BE                    QSUB 240    @I@@@@C DISCARDED, IS INVESTED ON WEFJ
)@@G@@LL BEHAVED PANELS. THE                    QSUB 250    @I@@@@C PROCESS ISFK
)@@G@@ COMPLETE WHEN NO CONVERGENCE FAILURE OCCURS ON             QSUB 260    FL
)@@G@@@I@@@@C ANY PANEL AND THE SUM OF THE RESULTS OBTAINED BY QUAD ON        FM
)@@G@@      QSUB 270    @I@@@@C EACH PANEL IS TAKEN AS THE VALUE OF THE INTEGRFN
)@@G@@AL.                     QSUB 280    @I@@@@C   THE PROCESS IS VERY CAUTIOFO
)@@G@@US IN THAT THE SUBDIVISION OF             QSUB 290    @I@@@@C THE INTERVFP
)@@G@@AL (A,B) IS UNIFORM, THE FINENESS OF WHICH IS               QSUB 300    FQ
)@@G@@@I@@@@C CONTROLLED BY THE SUCCESS OF QUAD.  IN THIS WAY IT IS           FR
)@@G@@      QSUB 310    @I@@@@C RATHER DIFFICULT FOR A SPURIOUS CONVERGENCE TOFS
)@@G@@ SLIP                   QSUB 320    @I@@@@C THROUGH.                    FT
)@@G@@                                          QSUB 330    @I@@@@C   THE CONVFU
)@@G@@ERGENCE CRITERION OF QUAD IS SLIGHTLY RELAXED               QSUB 340    FV
)@@G@@@I@@@@C IN THAT A PANEL IS DEEMED TO HAVE BEEN SUCCESSFULLY             FW
)@@G@@      QSUB 350    @I@@@@C INTEGRATED IF EITHER QUAD CONVERGES OR THE ESTFX
)@@G@@IMATED                  QSUB 360    @I@@@@C ABSOLUTE ERROR COMMITTED ON FY
)@@G@@THIS PANEL DOES NOT EXCEED                QSUB 370    @I@@@@C EPSIL TIMEFZ
)@@G@@S THE ESTIMATED ABSOLUTE VALUE OF THE INTEGRAL              QSUB 380    GA
)@@G@@@I@@@@C OVER (A,B).  THIS RELAXATION IS TO TRY TO TAKE ACCOUNT OF       GB
)@@G@@      QSUB 390    @I@@@@C A COMMON SITUATION WHERE ONE PARTICULAR PANEL GC
)@@G@@CAUSES                  QSUB 400    @I@@@@C SPECIAL DIFFICULTY, PERHAPS GD
)@@G@@DUE TO A SINGULARITY OF SOME              QSUB 410    @I@@@@C TYPE.  IN GE
)@@G@@THIS CASE QUAD COULD OBTAIN NEARLY EXACT                    QSUB 420    GF
)@@G@@@I@@@@C ANSWERS ON ALL OTHER PANELS AND SO THE RELATIVE ERROR FOR       GG
)@@G@@      QSUB 430    @I@@@@C THE TOTAL INTEGRATION WOULD BE ALMOST ENTIRELYGH
)@@G@@ DUE TO THE             QSUB 440    @I@@@@C DELINQUENT PANEL.  WITHOUT TGI
)@@G@@HIS CONDITION THE COMPUTATION             QSUB 450    @I@@@@C MIGHT CONTGJ
)@@G@@INUE DESPITE THE REQUESTED RELATIVE ERROR BEING             QSUB 460    GK
)@@G@@@I@@@@C ACHIEVED.                                                       GL
)@@G@@      QSUB 470    @I@@@@C   THE OUTCOME OF THE INTEGRATION IS INDICATED GM
)@@G@@BY ICHECK.              QSUB 480    @I@@@@C   ICHECK=0  -  CONVERGENCE OGN
)@@G@@BTAINED WITHOUT INVOKING                  QSUB 490    @I@@@@C           GO
)@@G@@     SUBDIVISION.  THIS CORRESPONDS TO THE                  QSUB 500    GP
)@@G@@@I@@@@C                DIRECT USE OF QUAD.                              GQ
)@@G@@      QSUB 510    @I@@@@C   ICHECK=1  -  RESULT OBTAINED AFTER INVOKING GR
)@@G@@SUBDIVISION.            QSUB 520    @I@@@@C   ICHECK=2  -  AS FOR ICHECKGS
)@@G@@=1 BUT AT SOME POINT THE                  QSUB 530    @I@@@@C           GT
)@@G@@     RELAXED CONVERGENCE CRITERION WAS USED.                QSUB 540    GU
)@@G@@@I@@@@C                THE RISK OF UNDERESTIMATING THE RELATIVE         GV
)@@G@@      QSUB 550    @I@@@@C                ERROR WILL BE INCREASED.  IF NEGW
)@@G@@CESSARY,                QSUB 560    @I@@@@C                CONFIDENCE MAGX
)@@G@@Y BE RESTORED BY CHECKING                 QSUB 570    @I@@@@C           GY
)@@G@@     EPSIL AND RELERR FOR A SERIOUS DISCREPANCY.            QSUB 580    GZ
)@@G@@@I@@@@C   ICHECK NEGATIVE                                               HA
)@@G@@      QSUB 590    @I@@@@C                IF DURING THE SUBDIVISION PROCEHB
)@@G@@SS THE                  QSUB 600    @I@@@@C                ALLOWED UPPERHC
)@@G@@ LIMIT ON THE NUMBER OF PANELS            QSUB 610    @I@@@@C           HD
)@@G@@     THAT MAY BE GENERATED (PRESENTLY 4096) IS              QSUB 620    HE
)@@G@@@I@@@@C                REACHED A RESULT IS OBTAINED WHICH MAY BE        HF
)@@G@@      QSUB 630    @I@@@@C                UNRELIABLE BY CONTINUING THE INHG
)@@G@@TEGRATION               QSUB 640    @I@@@@C                WITHOUT FURTHHH
)@@G@@ER SUBDIVISION IGNORING                   QSUB 650    @I@@@@C           HI
)@@G@@     CONVERGENCE FAILURES. THIS OCCURRENCE IS               QSUB 660    HJ
)@@G@@@I@@@@C                FLAGGED BY RETURNING ICHECK WITH NEGATIVE        HK
)@@G@@      QSUB 670    @I@@@@C                SIGN.                          HL
)@@G@@                        QSUB 680    @I@@@@C  THE RELIABILITY OF THE ALGOHM
)@@G@@RITHM WILL DECREASE FOR LARGE             QSUB 690    @I@@@@C  VALUES OFHN
)@@G@@ EPSIL.  IT IS RECOMMENDED THAT EPSIL SHOULD                QSUB 700    HO
)@@G@@@I@@@@C  GENERALLY BE LESS THAN ABOUT 0.001.                            HP
)@@G@@      QSUB 710    @I@@@@      DIMENSION RESULT(8)                       HQ
)@@G@@                        QSUB 720    @I@@@@      INTEGER BAD, OUT        HR
)@@G@@                                          QSUB 730    @I@@@@      LOGICAHS
)@@G@@L RHS                                                       QSUB 740    HT
)@@G@@@I@@@@      EXTERNAL F                                                  HU
)@@G@@      QSUB 750    @I@@@@      DATA NMAX/4096/                           HV
)@@G@@                        QSUB 760    @I@@@@      CALL NIX3PT (A, B, RESULHW
)@@G@@T, K, EPSIL, NPTS, ICHECK, F)             QSUB0770    @I@@@@      QSUB =HX
)@@G@@ RESULT(K)                                                  QSUB 780    HY
)@@G@@@I@@@@      RELERR = 0.0                                                HZ
)@@G@@      QSUB 790    @I@@@@      IF (QSUB.NE.0.0) RELERR =                 IA
)@@G@@                        QSUB 800    @I@@@@     * ABS((RESULT(K)-RESULT(KIB
)@@G@@-1))/QSUB)                                QSUB 810    @I@@@@C CHECK IF SIC
)@@G@@UBDIVISION IS NEEDED.                                       QSUB 820    ID
)@@G@@@I@@@@      IF (ICHECK.EQ.0) RETURN                                     IE
)@@G@@      QSUB 830    @I@@@@C SUBDIVIDE                                     IF
)@@G@@                        QSUB 840    @I@@@@      ESTIM = ABS(QSUB*EPSIL) IG
)@@G@@                                          QSUB 850    @I@@@@      IC = 1IH
)@@G@@                                                            QSUB 860    II
)@@G@@@I@@@@      RHS = .FALSE.                                               IJ
)@@G@@      QSUB 870    @I@@@@      N = 1                                     IK
)@@G@@                        QSUB 880    @I@@@@      H = B - A               IL
)@@G@@                                          QSUB 890    @I@@@@      BAD = IM
)@@G@@1                                                           QSUB 900    IN
)@@G@@@I@@@@   10 QSUB = 0.0                                                  IO
)@@G@@      QSUB 910    @I@@@@      RELERR = 0.0                              IP
)@@G@@                        QSUB 920    @I@@@@      H = H*0.5               IQ
)@@G@@                                          QSUB 930    @I@@@@      N = N IR
)@@G@@+ N                                                         QSUB 940    IS
)@@G@@@I@@@@C INTERVAL (A,B) DIVIDED INTO N EQUAL SUBINTERVALS.               IT
)@@G@@      QSUB 950    @I@@@@C INTEGRATE OVER SUBINTERVALS BAD TO (BAD+1) WHEIU
)@@G@@RE TROUBLE              QSUB 960    @I@@@@C HAS OCCURRED.               IV
)@@G@@                                          QSUB 970    @I@@@@      M1 = BIW
)@@G@@AD                                                          QSUB 980    IX
)@@G@@@I@@@@      M2 = BAD + 1                                                IY
)@@G@@      QSUB 990    @I@@@@      OUT = 1                                   IZ
)@@G@@                        QSUB1000    @I@@@@      GO TO 50                JA
)@@G@@                                          QSUB1010    @I@@@@C INTEGRATE JB
)@@G@@OVER SUBINTERVALS 1 TO (BAD-1)                              QSUB1020    JC
)@@G@@@I@@@@   20 M1 = 1                                                      JD
)@@G@@      QSUB1030    @I@@@@      M2 = BAD - 1                              JE
)@@G@@                        QSUB1040    @I@@@@      RHS = .FALSE.           JF
)@@G@@                                          QSUB1050    @I@@@@      OUT = JG
)@@G@@2                                                           QSUB1060    JH
)@@G@@@I@@@@      GO TO 50                                                    JI
)@@G@@      QSUB1070    @I@@@@C INTEGRATE OVER SUBINTERVALS (BAD+2) TO N.     JJ
)@@G@@                        QSUB1080    @I@@@@   30 M1 = BAD + 2            JK
)@@G@@                                          QSUB1090    @I@@@@      M2 = NJL
)@@G@@                                                            QSUB1100    JM
)@@G@@@I@@@@      OUT = 3                                                     JN
)@@G@@      QSUB1110    @I@@@@      GO TO 50                                  JO
)@@G@@                        QSUB1120    @I@@@@C SUBDIVISION RESULT          JP
)@@G@@                                          QSUB1130    @I@@@@   40 ICHECKJQ
)@@G@@ = IC                                                       QSUB1140    JR
)@@G@@@I@@@@      RELERR = RELERR/ABS(QSUB)                                   JS
)@@G@@      QSUB1150    @I@@@@      RETURN                                    JT
)@@G@@                        QSUB1160    @I@@@@C INTEGRATE OVER SUBINTERVALS JU
)@@G@@M1 TO M2.                                 QSUB1170    @I@@@@   50 IF (M1JV
)@@G@@.GT.M2) GO TO 90                                            QSUB1180    JW
)@@G@@@I@@@@      DO 80 JJ=M1,M2                                              JX
)@@G@@      QSUB1190    @I@@@@        J = JJ                                  JY
)@@G@@                        QSUB1200    @I@@@@C EXAMINE FIRST THE LEFT OR RIJZ
)@@G@@GHT HALF OF THE SUBDIVIDED                QSUB1210    @I@@@@C TROUBLESOMKA
)@@G@@E INTERVAL DEPENDING ON THE OBSERVED TREND.                 QSUB1220    KB
)@@G@@@I@@@@        IF (RHS) J = M2 + M1 - JJ                                 KC
)@@G@@      QSUB1230    @I@@@@        ALPHA = A + H*(J-1)                     KD
)@@G@@                        QSUB1240    @I@@@@        BETA = ALPHA + H      KE
)@@G@@                                          QSUB1250    @I@@[@      CALL NKF
)@@G@@IX3PT (ALPHA, BETA, RESULT, M, EPSIL, NF, ICHECK, F)        QSUB1260    KG
)@@G@@@I[@@@        COMP = ABS(RESULT(M)-RESULT(M-1))                         KH
)@@G@@      QSUB1270    @I@@@@        NPTS = NPTS + NF                        KI
)@@G@@                        QSUB1280    @I@@@@        IF (ICHECK.NE.1) GO TOKJ
)@@G@@ 70                                       QSUB1290    @I@@@@        IF (KK
)@@G@@COMP.LE.ESTIM) GO TO 100                                    QSUB1300    KL
)@@G@@@I@@@@C SUBINTERVAL J HAS CAUSED TROUBLE.                               KM
)@@G@@      QSUB1310    @I@@@@C CHECK IF FURTHER SUBDIVISION SHOULD BE CARRIEDKN
)@@G@@ OUT.                   QSUB1320    @I@@@@        IF (N.EQ.NMAX) GO TO 6KO
)@@G@@0                                         QSUB1330    @I@@@@        BAD KP
)@@G@@= 2*J - 1                                                   QSUB1340    KQ
)@@G@@@I@@@@        RHS = .FALSE.                                             KR
)@@G@@      QSUB1350    @I@@@@        IF ((J-2*(J/2)).EQ.0) RHS = .TRUE.      KS
)@@G@@                        QSUB1360    @I@@@@        GO TO 10              KT
)@@G@@                                          QSUB1370    @I@@@@   60   IC =KU
)@@G@@ -IABS(IC)                                                  QSUB1380    KV
)@@G@@@I@@@@   70   QSUB = QSUB + RESULT(M)                                   KW
)@@G@@      QSUB1390    @I@@@@   80 CONTINUE                                  KX
)@@G@@                        QSUB1400    @I@@@@      RELERR = RELERR + COMP  KY
)@@G@@                                          QSUB1410    @I@@@@   90 GO TO KZ
)@@G@@(20,30,40), OUT                                             QSUB1420    LA
)@@G@@@I@@@@C RELAXED CONVERGENCE                                             LB
)@@G@@      QSUB1430    @I@@@@  100 IC = ISIGN(2,IC)                          LC
)@@G@@                        QSUB1440    @I@@@@      GO TO 70                LD
)@@G@@                                          QSUB1450    @I@@@@      END   LE
)@@G@@                                                            QSUB1460    LF
)@@G@@___(M1  100 IC = ISIGN(2,IC)                                            LG
)@@G@@      QSUB1440    @I@@@@      GO TO 70          )@F@C@)@@[F]@K1#@@@@@@@@LH
)@@G@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@G@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@/,0@@@@@@[@@AA@@@A)@D[N#^GY0^GLI
)@@G@@^[#B?@C@[J_"R@K@@)/K@@@R(@@@@@A@K@@) @@@@@[@@@@@C@[J_"R@K@@G@[C@@XAB@@@ALJ
)@@G@@)@N[N;@[@K^[#@@@@@C@@@@@@[I@@X/K@@]7N@0@@V/K@@@W*@@@@@[@@@@@E@@@@G"G@@@@LK
)@@G@@"^[J_.AC@@@A)@X[M^G^GK1#@K0@@@[[@@@K" @@@@C[@@@@[@)@@J @@@@E[@)@@IC/)@@[LL

)@@G@@/K@@[K[[)@@DC.)@@[[[@@@MG.@@@[[[@@@LC[@@@CAF@@@A)@'[F#^G^GK[#^GK0@@@@@@@LO

)@@G@@@]@@@@            @@@@[^      ALPH=1.9140625                            OP
)@@G@@*[S@@@*SDFF*@I@@@@      SUBROUTINE NIMHSL (N, A, B, U, ISET, TOL, MAXSMPOQ
)@@G@@, MAXSEC, JOPT,   MHSL0010    @I@@@@     * VINT, ERR, NSAMP, IOUT, T0)  OR
)@@G@@                                    MHSL0020    @I@@@@C     SECOND LEVELOS
)@@G@@ ROUTINE FOR HASELGROVE'S METHOD                      MHSL0030    @I@@@@OT
)@@G@@      EXTERNAL U                                                        OU
)@@G@@MHSL0040    @I@@@@      INTEGER OFFSET                                  OV
)@@G@@                  MHSL0050    @I@@@@      DOUBLE PRECISION S1, S2, GEN, OW
)@@G@@Z                                   MHSL0060    @I@@@@      DIMENSION A(OX
)@@G@@1), B(1), C(8), D(8), DELTA(6), X(8), Z(8)            MHSL0070    @I@@@@OY
)@@G@@      COMMON /QUAD88/ GEN(72)                                           OZ
)@@G@@MHSL0080    @I@@@@C     GET GENERATING POINTS                           PA
)@@G@@                  MHSL0090    @I@@@@      CALL NIHS88                   PB
)@@G@@                                    MHSL0100    @I@@@@C     POINTER TO CPC
)@@G@@ORRECT SET OF GENERATOR POINTS                        MHSL0110    @I@@@@PD
)@@G@@      OFFSET= 36*(ISET-1) + (N*(N-1))/2                                 PE
)@@G@@MHSL0120    @I@@@@C     COMPUTE CENTER, WIDTH, AND TWICE THE VOLUME     PF
)@@G@@                  MHSL0130    @I@@@@      VOLMX2= 2.0                   PG
)@@G@@                                    MHSL0140    @I@@@@      DO 110 J= 1,PH
)@@G@@ N                                                    MHSL0150    @I@@@@PI
)@@G@@      VOLMX2= VOLMX2 * (B(J) - A(J))                                    PJ
)@@G@@MHSL0160    @I@@@@      C(J)= 0.5 * (A(J) + B(J))                       PK
)@@G@@                  MHSL0170    @I@@@@  110 D(J)= B(J) - A(J)             PL
)@@G@@                                    MHSL0180    @I@@@@C     INITIALIZATIPM
)@@G@@ONS                                                   MHSL0190    @I@@@@PN
)@@G@@      NSAMP= 0                                                          PO
)@@G@@MHSL0200    @I@@@@      S1= U(A)                                        PP
)@@G@@                  MHSL0210    @I@@@@      S2= S1                        PQ
)@@G@@                                    MHSL0220    @I@@@@      VINT1= 0.   PR
)@@G@@                                                      MHSL0230    @I@@@@PS
)@@G@@      DO 120 I= 1, 6                                                    PT
)@@G@@MHSL0240    @I@@@@  120 DELTA(I)= 1.E+35                                PU
)@@G@@                  MHSL0250    @I@@@@      DO 130 J= 1, N                PV
)@@G@@                                    MHSL0260    @I@@@@  130 Z(J)= 0.0D0 PW
)@@G@@                                                      MHSL0270    @I@@@@PX
)@@G@@      IF (JOPT .GE. 1) PRINT 800                                        PY
)@@G@@MHSL0280    @I@@@@C     TAKE A SAMPLE OF 100 POINTS                     PZ
)@@G@@                  MHSL0290    @I@@@@  200 NSAMP= NSAMP + 1              QA
)@@G@@                                    MHSL0300    @I@@@@      DO 230 I= 1,QB
)@@G@@ 100                                                  MHSL0310    @I@@@@QC
)@@G@@C     GET NEXT POINT                                                    QD
)@@G@@MHSL0320    @I@@@@      DO 220 J= 1, N                                  QE
)@@G@@                  MHSL0330    @I@@@@      Z(J)= Z(J) + GEN(OFFSET+J)    QF
)@@G@@                                    MHSL0340    @I@@@@      IF (Z(J) - 0QG
)@@G@@.5D0) 220, 220, 210                                   MHSL0350    @I@@@@QH
)@@G@@C     NORMALIZED POINT LIES IN (-1/2,+1/2)                              QI
)@@G@@MHSL0360    @I@@@@  210 Z(J)= Z(J) - 1.0D0                              QJ
)@@G@@                  MHSL0370    @I@@@@  220 X(J)= D(J)*Z(J) + C(J)        QK
)@@G@@                                    MHSL0380    @I@@@@C     UPDATE SUMS QL
)@@G@@                                                      MHSL0390    @I@@@@QM
)@@G@@      S1= S1 + U(X)                                                     QN
)@@G@@MHSL0400    @I@@@@  230 S2= S2 + S1                                     QO
)@@G@@                  MHSL0410    @I@@@@C     GET INTEGRAL ESTIMATE         QP
)@@G@@                                    MHSL0420    @I@@@@      P= (100*NSAMQQ
)@@G@@P + 1)**2                                             MHSL0430    @I@@@@QR
)@@G@@      VINT= VOLMX2 * S2 / P                                             QS
)@@G@@MHSL0440    @I@@@@C     GET 'ERROR ESTIMATE'.  USE TWICE THE AVERAGE OF QT
)@@G@@THE PREVIOUS 5    MHSL0450    @I@@@@C     'UNBIASED' ERROR ESTIMATES FORQU
)@@G@@ TESTING FOR CONVERGENCE.  FOR      MHSL0460    @I@@@@C     SMOOTH FUNCTQV
)@@G@@IONS, AN 'UNBIASED' ERROR ESTIMATE IS /I(M) - I/ =    MHSL0470    @I@@@@QW
)@@G@@C     /I(M) - I(M-1)/ * M/2.                                            QX
)@@G@@MHSL0480    @I@@@@      DELTA(6)= DELTA(5)                              QY
)@@G@@                  MHSL0490    @I@@@@      DELTA(5)= DELTA(4)            QZ
)@@G@@                                    MHSL0500    @I@@@@      DELTA(4)= DERA
)@@G@@LTA(3)                                                MHSL0510    @I@@@@RB
)@@G@@      DELTA(3)= DELTA(2)                                                RC
)@@G@@MHSL0520    @I@@@@      DELTA(2)= DELTA(1)                              RD
)@@G@@                  MHSL0530    @I@@@@      DELTA(1)= FLOAT(NSAMP) * ABS(VRE
)@@G@@INT - VINT1)                        MHSL0540    @I@@@@      VINT1= VINT RF
)@@G@@                                                      MHSL0550    @I@@@@RG
)@@G@@C     AT LEAST 6 SAMPLES ARE NEEDED                                     RH
)@@G@@MHSL0560    @I@@@@      IF (NSAMP - 6) 240, 250, 260                    RI
)@@G@@                  MHSL0570    @I@@@@  240 ERR= 1.E+35                   RJ
)@@G@@                                    MHSL0580    @I@@@@      GO TO 270   RK
)@@G@@                                                      MHSL0590    @I@@@@RL
)@@G@@  250 ERR= 0.                                                           RM
)@@G@@MHSL0600    @I@@@@      DO 255 I= 1, 5                                  RN
)@@G@@                  MHSL0610    @I@@@@  255 ERR= ERR + DELTA(I)           RO
)@@G@@                                    MHSL0620    @I@@@@      ERR= 0.2*ERRRP
)@@G@@                                                      MHSL0630    @I@@@@RQ
)@@G@@      GO TO 270                                                         RR
)@@G@@MHSL0640    @I@@@@  260 ERR= ERR + 0.2*(DELTA(1)-DELTA(6))              RS
)@@G@@                  MHSL0650    @I@@@@  270 T1= .001 * (TIMEF(P) - T0)    RT
)@@G@@                                    MHSL0660    @I@@@@C     PRINT IF REQRU
)@@G@@UESTED                                                MHSL0670    @I@@@@RV
)@@G@@      IF (JOPT .LE. 0) GO TO 300                                        RW
)@@G@@MHSL0680    @I@@@@      IF (MOD(NSAMP,JOPT) .EQ. 0) PRINT 801, NSAMP, VIRX
)@@G@@NT, ERR, T1       MHSL0690    @I@@@@C     CHECK TOLERANCE               RY
)@@G@@                                    MHSL0700    @I@@@@  300 IF (ERR .GT.RZ
)@@G@@ ABS(TOL*VINT)) GO TO 310                             MHSL0710    @I@@@@SA
)@@G@@      IOUT= 1                                                           SB
)@@G@@MHSL0720    @I@@@@      GO TO 400                                       SC
)@@G@@                  MHSL0730    @I@@@@C     CHECK SAMPLE SIZE             SD
)@@G@@                                    MHSL0740    @I@@@@  310 IF (NSAMP .LSE
)@@G@@T. MAXSMP) GO TO 320                                  MHSL0750    @I@@@@SF
)@@G@@      IOUT= 2                                                           SG
)@@G@@MHSL0760    @I@@@@      GO TO 400                                       SH
)@@G@@                  MHSL0770    @I@@@@C     CHECK TIME                    SI
)@@G@@                                    MHSL0780    @I@@@@  320 NSEC= T1    SJ
)@@G@@                                                      MHSL0790    @I@@@@SK
)@@G@@      IF (NSEC .LT. MAXSEC) GO TO 200                                   SL
)@@G@@MHSL0800    @I@@@@      IOUT= 3                                         SM
)@@G@@                  MHSL0810    @I@@@@C     END OF SAMPLING, PRINT LAST ONSN
)@@G@@E IF REQUESTED                      MHSL0820    @I@@@@  400 IF (JOPT .LESO
)@@G@@. 0) GO TO 500                                        MHSL0830    @I@@@@SP
)@@G@@      IF (MOD(NSAMP,JOPT) .NE. 0) PRINT 801, NSAMP, VINT, ERR, T1       SQ
)@@G@@MHSL0840    @I@@@@  500 RETURN                                          SR
)@@G@@                  MHSL0850    @I@@@@  800 FORMAT (1H0, 34X, 'SAMPLE INFOSS
)@@G@@RMATION' / 1H0, 19X, 'SAMPLE',      MHSL0860    @I@@@@     * 7X, 'INTEGRST
)@@G@@AL', 10X, 'ERROR', 9X, 'ELAPSED' / 1H , 20X,          MHSL0870    @I@@@@SU
)@@G@@     * 'SIZE', 8X, 'ESTIMATE', 8X, 'ESTIMATE', 10X, 'TIME')             SV
)@@G@@MHSL0880    @I@@@@  801 FORMAT (1H , 11X, I11, '00', 2E16.6, F15.3)     SW
)@@G@@                  MHSL0890    @I@@@@      END                           SX
)@@G@@                                    MHSL0900    ___255 I= 1, 5          SY
)@@G@@                                          MHSL0610    @I@@@@  255 ERR= ESZ
)@@G@@RR + DELTA(I)           )@@[M^GCKK0CSK0@@@C/)@@[;K@@@[T@@@[2H@@@[2C/@@@[TA
