)@@G@@*[S@@@*SDFF*@I@@@@      SUBROUTINE NIMCSL (N, A, B, FUNEX, MESH, TOL, MAUV
)@@G@@XSMP, MAXSEC,     MCSL0010    @I@@@@     * JOPT, VINT, STE, NSAMP, IOUT,UW
)@@G@@ C, D, X, T0)                       MCSL0020    @I@@@@C     SECOND LEVELUX
)@@G@@ ROUTINE FOR TSUDA'S MONTE CARLO METHOD               MCSL0030    @I@@@@UY
)@@G@@      EXTERNAL FUNEX                                                    UZ
)@@G@@MCSL0040    @I@@@@      DIMENSION A(1), B(1), C(1), D(1), X(1), P(50)   VA
)@@G@@                  MCSL0050    @I@@@@      COMMON /QUAD50/ V(275), W(275)VB
)@@G@@                                    MCSL0060    @I@@@@C     GET WEIGHTS VC
)@@G@@AND NODES                                             MCSL0070    @I@@@@VD
)@@G@@      CALL NICH50                                                       VE
)@@G@@MCSL0080    @I@@@@C     COMPUTE CENTER, WIDTH, VOLUME                   VF
)@@G@@                  MCSL0090    @I@@@@      VOLUME= 1.                    VG
)@@G@@                                    MCSL0100    @I@@@@      DO 110 J= 1,VH
)@@G@@ N                                                    MCSL0110    @I@@@@VI
)@@G@@      C(J)= (B(J)+A(J))/2.                                              VJ
)@@G@@MCSL0120    @I@@@@      D(J)= (B(J)-A(J))/2.                            VK
)@@G@@                  MCSL0130    @I@@@@  110 VOLUME= VOLUME*D(J)*2.        VL
)@@G@@                                    MCSL0140    @I@@@@C     SET UP POINTVM
)@@G@@ER FOR CORRECT SET OF WEIGHTS                         MCSL0150    @I@@@@VN
)@@G@@      K0= 1 + MESH*(MESH-5)/10                                          VO
)@@G@@MCSL0160    @I@@@@C     SET UP CUMULATIVE PROBABILITIES FOR DISCRETE RANVP
)@@G@@DOM GENERATOR     MCSL0170    @I@@@@      K1= K0                        VQ
)@@G@@                                    MCSL0180    @I@@@@      P(1)= W(K1)/VR
)@@G@@2.                                                    MCSL0190    @I@@@@VS
)@@G@@      DO 120 K= 2, MESH                                                 VT
)@@G@@MCSL0200    @I@@@@      K1= K1 + 1                                      VU
)@@G@@                  MCSL0210    @I@@@@  120 P(K)= P(K-1) + W(K1)/2.       VV
)@@G@@                                    MCSL0220    @I@@@@C     INITIALIZATIVW
)@@G@@ONS                                                   MCSL0230    @I@@@@VX
)@@G@@      NSAMP= 0                                                          VY
)@@G@@MCSL0240    @I@@@@      SUM= 0.                                         VZ
)@@G@@                  MCSL0250    @I@@@@      SUMSQ= 0.                     WA
)@@G@@                                    MCSL0260    @I@@@@      IF (JOPT .GEWB
)@@G@@. 1) PRINT 800                                        MCSL0270    @I@@@@WC
)@@G@@C     TAKE A SAMPLE OF 1000 POINTS                                      WD
)@@G@@MCSL0280    @I@@@@  200 NSAMP= NSAMP + 1                                WE
)@@G@@                  MCSL0290    @I@@@@      DO 220 I= 1, 1000             WF
)@@G@@                                    MCSL0300    @I@@@@C     GET A POINT WG
)@@G@@                                                      MCSL0310    @I@@@@WH
)@@G@@      DO 210 J= 1, N                                                    WI
)@@G@@MCSL0320    @I@@@@  210 X(J)= C(J) + D(J)*RANDS(V(K0), P, MESH)         WJ
)@@G@@                  MCSL0330    @I@@@@      Y= FUNEX(X)                   WK
)@@G@@                                    MCSL0340    @I@@@@C     UPDATE SUM AWL
)@@G@@ND SUM OF SQUARES                                     MCSL0350    @I@@@@WM
)@@G@@      SUM= SUM + Y                                                      WN
)@@G@@MCSL0360    @I@@@@  220 SUMSQ= SUMSQ + Y**2                             WO
)@@G@@                  MCSL0370    @I@@@@C     GET ESTIMATE OF INTEGRAL AND SWP
)@@G@@TANDARD ERROR                       MCSL0380    @I@@@@      S= 1000 * NSWQ
)@@G@@AMP                                                   MCSL0390    @I@]@@WR
)@@G@@      VINT= VOLUME * SUM / S                                            WS
)@@G@@MCSL0400    @I@]@@      STE= VOLUME * SQRT((SUMSQ - S*VINT**2)/(S*(S-1))WT
)@@G@@)                 MCSL0410    @I@@@]      AVER= SUM / S                 WU
)@@G@@                                    MCSL0400    @I@@@]      STE= VOLUME WV
)@@G@@* SQRT((SUMSQ - S*AVER**2)/(S*(S-1)))                 MCSL0410    @I@@@]WW
)@@G@@      VINT= VOLUME * AVER                                               WX
)@@G@@MCSL0415    @I@@@@      T1=(TIMEF(S) - T0) * .001                       WY
)@@G@@                  MCSL0420    @I@@@@C     PRINT IF REQUESTED            WZ
)@@G@@                                    MCSL0430    @I@@@@      IF (JOPT .LEXA
)@@G@@. 0) GO TO 300                                        MCSL0440    @I@@@@XB
)@@G@@      IF (MOD(NSAMP,JOPT) .EQ. 0) PRINT 801, NSAMP, VINT, STE, T1       XC
)@@G@@MCSL0450    @I@@@@C     CHECK TOLERANCE                                 XD
)@@G@@                  MCSL0460    @I@@@@  300 IF (STE .GT. ABS(TOL*VINT)) GOXE
)@@G@@ TO 310                             MCSL0470    @I@@@@      IOUT= 1     XF
)@@G@@                                                      MCSL0480    @I@@@@XG
)@@G@@      GO TO 400                                                         XH
)@@G@@MCSL0490    @I@@@@C     CHECK SAMPLE SIZE                               XI
)@@G@@                  MCSL0500    @I@@@@  310 IF (NSAMP .LT. MAXSMP) GO TO 3XJ
)@@G@@20                                  MCSL0510    @I@@@@      IOUT= 2     XK
)@@G@@                                                      MCSL0520    @I@@@@XL
)@@G@@      GO TO 400                                                         XM
)@@G@@MCSL0530    @I@@@@C     CHECK TIME                                      XN
)@@G@@                  MCSL0540    @I@#@@  320 NSEC= T1                      XO
)@@G@@                                    MCSL0550    @I@@[#  320 IF (MAXSEC .XP
)@@G@@EQ. 'NONE') GO TO 200                                 MCSL0550    @I@@[#XQ
)@@G@@      NSEC= T1                                                          XR
)@@G@@MCSL0555    @I[@@@      IF (NSEC .LT. MAXSEC) GO TO 200                 XS
)@@G@@                  MCSL0560    @I@@@@      IOUT= 3                       XT
)@@G@@                                    MCSL0570    @I@@@@C     END OF SAMPLXU
)@@G@@ING, PRINT LAST ONE IF REQUESTED                      MCSL0580    @I@@@@XV
)@@G@@  400 IF (JOPT .LE. 0) GO TO 500                                        XW
)@@G@@MCSL0590    @I@[@@      IF (MOD(NSAMP,JOUT) .NE. 0) PRINT 801, NSAMP, VIXX
)@@G@@NT, STE, T1       MCSL0600    @I@@@[      IF (MOD(NSAMP,JOPT) .NE. 0) PRXY
)@@G@@INT 801, NSAMP, VINT, STE, T1       MCSL0600    @I@@@@  500 RETURN      XZ
)@@G@@                                                      MCSL0610    @I@[@@YA
)@@G@@  800 FORMAT (1H0, 30X, 'SAMPLE INFORMATION' / 1H0, 19X, 'SAMPLE',      YB
)@@G@@MCSL0620    @I@@@[  800 FORMAT (1H0, 34X, 'SAMPLE INFORMATION' / 1H0, 19YC
)@@G@@X, 'SAMPLE',      MCSL0620    @I@@@@     * 7X, 'INTEGRAL', 7X, 'STANDARDYD
)@@G@@', 8X, 'ELAPSED' / 1H , 20X,        MCSL0630    @I@@@@     * 'SIZE', 8X,YE
)@@G@@ 'ESTIMATE', 9X, 'ERROR', 11X, 'TIME')                MCSL0640    @I@@@@YF
)@@G@@  801 FORMAT (1H , 10X, I11, ',000', 2E15.5, F15.3)                     YG
)@@G@@MCSL0650    @I@@@@      END                                             YH
)@@G@@                  MCSL0660    ___T= VOLUME * AVER                       YI
)@@G@@                        MCSL0415    @I@@@@      T1=(TIMEF(S) - T0) * .00YJ

)@@G@@SUBROUTINE NIGAUS (F, A, B, NP, IOPT, VINT, $)                    GAUS00AD
)@@G@@10    @I@@@@      EXTERNAL F                                            AE
)@@G@@            GAUS0020    @I@@@@      DIMENSION QTYPE(2,4), X(2040)       AF
)@@G@@                              GAUS0030    @I@@@@      COMMON /QUAD01/ R(AG
)@@G@@100), W(100) /QUAD02/ RT(100), WT(100)          GAUS0040    @I@@@@      AH
)@@G@@DATA NCALL, NPX, NTYPEX, PI, SQPI, QTYPE /3*0, 3.14159265359,     GAUS00AI
)@@G@@50    @I@@@@     * 1.77245385091,' LEGENDRE QU LAGUERRE QU LAGUERRE QU  AJ
)@@G@@HERMITE QU'/GAUS0060    @I@@@@C     ************************************AK
)@@G@@******************************GAUS0070    @I@@@@C     NUMERICAL INTEGRATAL
)@@G@@ION OF F(X)DX OVER A FINITE, SINGLY INFINITE,   GAUS0080    @I@@@@C     AM
)@@G@@OR DOUBLY INFINITE INTEGRAL USING SIMPLE GAUSSIAN QUADRATURE      GAUS00AN
)@@G@@90    @I@@@@C     OF ORDER UP TO 100.                                   AO
)@@G@@            GAUS0100    @I@@@@C     ************************************AP
)@@G@@******************************GAUS0110    @I@@@@C     F      = NAME OF FAQ
)@@G@@UNCTION TO BE INTEGRATED.                       GAUS0120    @I@@@@C     AR
)@@G@@A      = LOWER LIMIT OF INTEGRATION, 'INF' MEANS MINUS INFINITY.  GAUS01AS
)@@G@@30    @I@@@@C     B      = UPPER LIMIT OF INTEGRATION, 'INF' MEANS PLUS AT
)@@G@@INFINITY.   GAUS0140    @I@@@@C     NP     = QUADRATURE ORDER.          AU
)@@G@@                              GAUS0150    @I@@@@C     IOPT   = OPTION TOAV
)@@G@@ CONTROL FINAL FINAL OUTPUT.                    GAUS0190    @I@@@@C     AW
)@@G@@         =0 ... SUPPRESS.                                         GAUS02AX
)@@G@@00    @I@@@@C              =1 ... PRINT.                                AY
)@@G@@            GAUS0210    @I@@@@C     VINT   = COMPUTED INTEGRAL VALUE.   AZ
)@@G@@                              GAUS0215    @I@@@@C     $K     = RETURN TOBA
)@@G@@ STATEMENT K IF ERRORS OCCURED.                 GAUS0220    @I@@@@C     BB
)@@G@@******************************************************************GAUS02BC
)@@G@@30    @I@@@@      T0= TIMEF(0.)                                         BD
)@@G@@            GAUS0240    @I@@@@C     CHECK NO. PARAMETERS.               BE
)@@G@@                              GAUS0250    @I@@@@      CALL URXITP(7)    BF
)@@G@@                                                GAUS0260    @I@@@@C     BG
)@@G@@CHECK FOR WARNINGS AND ERRORS.                                    GAUS02BH
)@@G@@70    @I@@@@      IERR= -1                                              BI
)@@G@@            GAUS0280    @I@@@@C     CHECK IF F IS A FUNCTION.           BJ
)@@G@@                              GAUS0290    @I@@@@      INCODE= FLD(0,6,F)BK
)@@G@@                                                GAUS0300    @I@@@@      BL
)@@G@@IF (INCODE .NE. 0 .AND. INCODE .NE. 63) GO TO 10                  GAUS03BM
)@@G@@10    @I@@@@      PRINT 911                                             BN
)@@G@@            GAUS0320    @I@@@@      IERR= 1                             BO
)@@G@@                              GAUS0330    @I@@@@C     CHECK IF NP IS 1 TBP
)@@G@@O 100.                                          GAUS0340    @I@@@@   10 BQ
)@@G@@IF (NP .GE. 1 .AND. NP .LE. 100) GO TO 20                         GAUS03BR
)@@G@@50    @I@@@@      PRINT 912, NP                                         BS
)@@G@@            GAUS0360    @I@@@@      IERR= 1                             BT
)@@G@@                              GAUS0370    @I@@@@C     CHECK IOPT (DEFAULBU
)@@G@@T=1).                                           GAUS0380    @I@@@@   20 BV
)@@G@@IF (IOPT .EQ. 0 .OR. IOPT .EQ. 1) GO TO 40                        GAUS04BW
)@@G@@20    @I@@@@      PRINT 922, IOPT                                       BX
)@@G@@            GAUS0430    @I@@@@      IERR= MAX(0,IERR)                   BY
)@@G@@                              GAUS0440    @I@]@@C     PRINT WALKBACK IF BZ
)@@G@@WARNINGS OR ERRORS OCCURED.                     GAUS0450    @I@]@@   40 CA
)@@G@@IF (IERR .EQ. -1) GO TO 50                                        GAUS04CB
)@@G@@60    @I@]@@      PRINT 900                                             CC
)@@G@@            GAUS0470    @I@]@@      CALL URWALK ('NIGAUS', 0)           CD
)@@G@@                              GAUS0480    @I^@@@C     TERMINATE IF ERRORCE
)@@G@@S OCCURED.                                      GAUS0490    @I@]@@      CF
)@@G@@IF (IERR .EQ. 1) GO TO 300                                        GAUS05CG
)@@G@@00    @I@@[]   40 IF (IERR) 50, 45, 300                                 CH
)@@G@@            GAUS0495    @I@@[]   45 PRINT 900                           CI
)@@G@@                              GAUS0500    @I@@[]      CALL URWALK ('NIGACJ
)@@G@@US', 0)                                         GAUS0505    @I[@@@C     CK
)@@G@@ASSIGN FILE WITH ROOTS AND WEIGHTS IF FIRST CALL.                 GAUS05CL
)@@G@@10    @I@@@@   50 IF (NCALL) 51, 51, 52                                 CM
)@@G@@            GAUS0520    @I@@@@   51 CALL ERTRAN (6, '@ASG,AX NIQUAD*DATACN
)@@G@@TABLE. . ')                   GAUS0530    @I@@@@      CALL ERTRAN (6, '@CO
)@@G@@USE  8,NIQUAD*DATATABLE. . ')                   GAUS0540    @I@@@@   52 CP
)@@G@@NCALL= NCALL + 1                                                  GAUS05CQ
)@@G@@50    @I@@@@      WTSUM= 0.0                                            CR
)@@G@@            GAUS0560    @I@@@@      SUMT= 0.0                           CS
)@@G@@                              GAUS0570    @I@@@@C     DETERMINE TYPE OF CT
)@@G@@QUADRATURE.                                     GAUS0580    @I@@@@      CU
)@@G@@NTYPE= 1                                                          GAUS05CV
)@@G@@90    @I@@@@      IF (A .EQ. 'INF') NTYPE= NTYPE + 1                    CW
)@@G@@            GAUS0600    @I@@@@      IF (B .EQ. 'INF') NTYPE= NTYPE + 2  CX
)@@G@@                              GAUS0610    @I@@@@C     DETERMINE IF NEW SCY

)@@G@@                  MCMC0510    @I[@@C      SUBROUTINE NIMCMC (N, A, B, U,ZH
)@@G@@ NP, EPS, NSAMP, NSEC,              MCMC0010    @I@@@C     * IOPT, JOPT,ZI
)@@G@@ VINT, ERR, IOUT, $)                                  MCMC0020    @I@@@CZJ
)@@G@@      EXTERNAL U                                                        ZK
)@@G@@MCMC0030    @I@@@C      DIMENSION A(1), B(1), TEXT(3), S(100), C(100), DZL
)@@G@@(100)             MCMC0040    @I@@@CC     ******************************ZM
)@@G@@************************************MCMC0050    @I@@@CC     APPROXIMATE ZN
)@@G@@NUMERICAL INTEGRATION OVER AN N-DIMENSIONAL           MCMC0060    @I@@@CZO
)@@G@@C     HYPERBRICK, A .LE. X .LE. B, USING TSUDA'S MONTE CARLO METHOD     ZP
)@@G@@MCMC0070    @I@@@CC     WHICH SAMPLES FROM CHEVYSHEFF POINTS.  THE QUADRZQ
)@@G@@ATURE ORDER       MCMC0080    @I@@@CC     SPECIFIED MAY BE 5 TO 50 IN MUZR
)@@G@@LTIPLES OF 5 AND SAMPLES OF 1000    MCMC0090    @I@@@CC     POINTS ARE TZS
)@@G@@AKEN UNTIL EITHER THE RELATIVE STANDARD ERROR IS      MCMC0100    @I@@@CZT
)@@G@@C     SMALL ENOUGH OR THE SAMPLE OR TIME LIMIT IS REACHED.              ZU
)@@G@@MCMC0110    @I@@@CC     NIMCMC WILL ACCEPT UP TO 100 DIMENSIONS.  NIMCMCZV
)@@G@@                  MCMC0120    @I@@@CC     IS NOT RECOMMENDED IF THE DIMEZW
)@@G@@NSIONALITY IS LOW (LESS THAN 4 OR 5)MCMC0130    @I@@@CC     BECAUSE OTHEZX
)@@G@@R ROUTINES ARE MORE ACCURATE AND EFFICIENT.  FOR      MCMC0140    @I@@@CZY
)@@G@@C     MONTE CARLO METHODS, 3 SIGNIFICANT DIGITS IS PAR.                 ZZ
)@@G@@MCMC0150    @I@@@CC     ************************************************AA
)@@G@@******************MCMC0160    @I@@@CC     N      = DIMENSIONALITY       AB
)@@G@@                                    MCMC0170    @I@@@CC     A      = ARRAC
)@@G@@AY OF LOWER LIMITS OF INTEGRATION REGION              MCMC0180    @I@@@CAD
)@@G@@C     B      = ARRAY OF UOWER LIMITS OF INTEGRATION REGION              AE
)@@G@@MCMC0190    @I@@@CC     U      = NAME OF FUNCTION TO BE INTEGRATED      AF
)@@G@@                  MCMC0200    @I@@@CC     NP     = QUADRATURE ORDER.  MAAG
)@@G@@Y BE 5,10,15, ..., OR 50            MCMC0210    @I@@@CC     EPS    = RELAH
)@@G@@ATIVE TOLERANCE FOR STANDARD ERROR                    MCMC0220    @I@@@CAI
)@@G@@C     NSAMP  = MAXIMUM NO. OF SAMPLES OF 1000 POINTS TO BE TAKEN        AJ
)@@G@@MCMC0230    @I@@@CC     NSEC   = TIME LIMIT IN SECONDS                  AK
)@@G@@                  MCMC0240    @I@@@CC     IOPT   = OPTION TO CONTROL FINAL
)@@G@@AL OUTPUT                           MCMC0250    @I@@@CC              =0 AM
)@@G@@... SUPPRESS OUTPUT                                   MCMC0260    @I@@@CAN
)@@G@@C              =1 ... PRINT FINAL OUTPUT                                AO
)@@G@@MCMC0270    @I@@@CC              =2 ... PRINT FINAL OUTPUT AND START ON AP
)@@G@@NEW PAGE          MCMC0280    @I@@@CC     JOPT   = FREQUENCY IN 1000S OFAQ
)@@G@@ POINTS TO OUTPUT SAMPLE            MCMC0293    @I@@@CC              INFAR
)@@G@@ORMATION, IF ZERO, THIS OUTPUT IS SUPPRESSED          MCMC0296    @I@@@CAS
)@@G@@C     VINT   = COMPUTED ESTIMATE OF INTEGRAL                            AT
)@@G@@MCMC0300    @I@@@CC     ERR    = STANDARD ERROR OF ESTIMATE             AU
)@@G@@                  MCMC0310    @I@@@CC     IOUT   = STATUS CODE          AV
)@@G@@                                    MCMC0330    @I@@@CC              =1 AW
)@@G@@... CONVERGENCE CRITERION MET                         MCMC0350    @I@@@CAX
)@@G@@C              =2 ... REACHED SAMPLE LIMIT, C. C. NOT MET               AY
)@@G@@MCMC0360    @I@@@CC              =3 ... REACHED TIME LIMIT, C. C. NOT MEAZ
)@@G@@T                 MCMC0370    @I@@@CC              =4 ... ERRORS OCCUREDBA
)@@G@@ IN CALLING SEQUENCE                MCMC0375    @I@@@CC     $K     = RETBB
)@@G@@URN TO STATEMENT K IF IOUT IS NOT 1                   MCMC0390    @I@@@CBC
)@@G@@C     ******************************************************************BD
)@@G@@MCMC0400    @I@@@C      DATA NCALL, TEXT /0, ' IS  ', 2*' NOT '/        BE
)@@G@@                  MCMC0410    @I@@@C      NCALL= NCALL + 1              BF
)@@G@@                                    MCMC0420    @I@@@CC     CHECK NO. PABG
)@@G@@RAMETERS                                              MCMC0425    @I@@@CBH
)@@G@@      CALL URXITP(14)                                                   BI

)@@G@@                  MCMC0435    @I@@@C      IOUT= -1                      BK
)@@G@@                                    MCMC0440    @I@@@CC     CHECK IF U IBL
)@@G@@S A FUNCTION                                          MCMC0445    @I@@@CBM
)@@G@@      INCODE= FLD(0, 6, U)                                              BN
)@@G@@MCMC0450    @I@@@C      IF (INCODE .NE. 0 .AND. INCODE .NE. 63) GO TO 10BO
)@@G@@0                 MCMC0455    @I@@@C      PRINT 911                     BP
)@@G@@                                    MCMC0460    @I@@@C      IOUT= 4     BQ
)@@G@@                                                      MCMC0465    @I@@@CBR
)@@G@@C     CHECK N, NSEC, NP, EPS, NSAMP, IOPT                               BS
)@@G@@MCMC0470    @I@@@C  100 IF (N .GE. 1 .AND. N .LE. 100) GO TO 105        BT
)@@G@@                  MCMC0475    @I@@@C      PRINT 912, N                  BU
)@@G@@                                    MCMC0480    @I@@@C      IOUT= 4     BV
)@@G@@                                                      MCMC0485    @I@@@CBW

)@@G@@(NP, 5), 50)                                          MCMC0505    @I@F@CCB
)@@G@@      NPV= 5*((NP+2)/5)                                                 CC

)@@G@@                  MCMC0510    @I@@@C      IF (NPV .EQ. NP) GO TO 115    CE

)@@G@@P, NPV                                                MCMC0520    @I@@@CCG
)@@G@@      IOUT= MAX(0,IOUT)                                                 CH
)@@G@@MCMC0525    @I@@@C  115 EPSV= EPS                                       CI

)@@G@@                                    MCMC0535    @I@@@C      EPSV= .005  CK

)@@G@@                                    MCMC0575    @I@@@C  125 IF (IOPT .GECU
)@@G@@. 0 .AND. IOPT .LE. 2) GO TO 130                      MCMC0580    @I@@@CCV
)@@G@@      PRINT 924, IOPT                                                   CW
)@@G@@MCMC0585    @I@@@C      IOUT= MAX (0, IOUT)                             CX
)@@G@@                  MCMC0590    @I@D@CC     PRINT WALKBACK IF WARNINGS OR CY
)@@G@@ERRORS OCCURED                      MCMC0595    @I@D@C  130 IF (IOUT .EQCZ
)@@G@@. -1) GO TO 135                                       MCMC0600    @I@D@CDA
)@@G@@      PRINT 906                                                         DB
)@@G@@MCMC0605    @I@@@DC     TERMINATE IF ERRORS OCCURED                     DC
)@@G@@                  MCMC0595    @I@@@D  130 IF (IOUT) 135, 132, 600       DD

)@@G@@                                                      MCMC0605    @I@@@CDF
)@@G@@      CALL URWALK ('NIMCMC', 0)                                         DG
)@@G@@MCMC0610    @I@D@CC     TERMINATE IF ERRORS OCCURED                     DH
)@@G@@                  MCMC0615    @I@D@C      IF (IOUT .EQ. 4) GO TO 600    DI
)@@G@@                                    MCMC0620    @I@@@CC     GET SEED FORDJ

)@@G@@  135 CALL NICLCK (MS)                                                  DL
)@@G@@MCMC0665    @I@@@C      ISEED= 100*MS + 10000000027                     DM
)@@G@@                  MCMC0667    @I@@@C  150 CALL RANDSS (ISEED)           DN
)@@G@@                                    MCMC0669    @I@@@CC     PRINT IF REQDO
)@@G@@UESTED                                                MCMC0700    @I@@@CDP
)@@G@@      IF (IOPT) 200, 300, 200                                           DQ

)@@G@@                                                      MCMC0750    @I@@@CDU
)@@G@@      PRINT 903, (J, A(J), B(J), J= 1, N)                               DV
)@@G@@MCMC0760    @I@@@CC     SOLVE USING SECOND LEVEL ROUTINE                DW
)@@G@@                  MCMC0770    @I@@@C  300 T0= TIMEF(0.)                 DX
)@@G@@                                    MCMC0780    @I@@@C      CALL NIMCSL DY
)@@G@@(N, A, B, U, NPV, EPSV, NSAMPV, NSEC,  JOPT,          MCMC0790    @I@@@CDZ

)@@G@@SUBROUTINE NIDCAR (F, A, B, TOL, IOPT, VINT, ERR, IOUT, $)        DCAR00KM
)@@G@@10    @I@@@@      EXTERNAL F                                            KN
)@@G@@            DCAR0020    @I@@@@      DIMENSION ITEXT(3,3), ITAB(5)       KO
)@@G@@                              DCAR0030    @I@@@@      DATA NCALL, ITEXT KP
)@@G@@/0, '   INTEGRATION NOT', '    INTEGRATION IS', DCAR0040    @I@@@@     *KQ
)@@G@@ 'INTEGRATION MAY BE'/                                            DCAR00KR
)@@G@@50    @I@@@@      DATA ITAB /2, 2 , 3, 1, 1/                            KS
)@@G@@            DCAR0055    @I@@@@C     ************************************KT
)@@G@@******************************DCAR0060    @I@@@@C     NUMERICAL INTEGRATKU
)@@G@@ION OF F(X)DX OVER (A,B) USING DEBOOR'S         DCAR0070    @I@@@@C     KV
)@@G@@CAUTIOUS ADAPTIVE ROMBERG INTEGRATION METHOD.                     DCAR00KW
)@@G@@80    @I@@@@C     ******************************************************KX
)@@G@@************DCAR0090    @I@@@@C     F      = NAME OF FUNCTION TO BE INTEKY
)@@G@@GRATED                        DCAR0100    @I@@@@C     A      = LOWER LIMKZ
)@@G@@IT OF INTEGRATION                               DCAR0110    @I@@@@C     LA
)@@G@@B      = UPPER LIMIT OF INTEGRATION                               DCAR01LB
)@@G@@20    @I@@@@C     TOL    = RELATIVE ACCURACY DESIRED IF POSITIVE, OR MINLC
)@@G@@US THE      DCAR0130    @I@@@@C              ABSOLUTE ACCURACY DESIRED ILD
)@@G@@F NEGATIVE.                   DCAR0140    @I@@@@C     IOPT   = OUTPUT OPLE
)@@G@@TION                                            DCAR0150    @I@@[@C     LF
)@@G@@       = -1 ... SUPPRESS RESULTS AND WARNINGS DURING COMPUTATION  DCAR01LG
)@@G@@52    @I@@[@C            =  0 ... SUPPRESS RESULTS AND PRINT WARNINGS DULH
)@@G@@RING COMP.  DCAR0155    @I@@[@C            =  1 ... PRINT RESULTS AND WALI
)@@G@@RNINGS DURING COMPUTATION     DCAR0158    @I@@@@C     VINT   = COMPUTED LJ
)@@G@@ESTIMATE OF INTEGRAL                            DCAR0160    @I@@@@C     LK
)@@G@@ERR    = COMPUTED ESTIMATE OF ERROR                               DCAR01LL
)@@G@@70    @I@@@@C     IOUT   = STATUS CODE                                  LM
)@@G@@            DCAR0180    @I@@@@C     $K     = RETURN TO STATEMENT K IF IOLN
)@@G@@UT EXCEEDS 3                  DCAR0190    @I@@@@C     ******************LO
)@@G@@************************************************DCAR0200    @I@@@@      LP
)@@G@@T0= TIMEF(0.)                                                     DCAR02LQ
)@@G@@10    @I@@@@      NCALL= NCALL + 1                                      LR
)@@G@@            DCAR0220    @I@@@@C     CHECK NO. PARAMETERS                LS
)@@G@@                              DCAR0230    @I@@@@      CALL URXITP(9)    LT
)@@G@@                                                DCAR0233    @I@@@@C     LU
)@@G@@CHECK FOR WARNINGS AND ERRORS                                     DCAR02LV
)@@G@@36    @I@@@@      IOUT= -1                                              LW
)@@G@@            DCAR0240    @I@@@@C     CHECK IF F IS A FUNCTION            LX

)@@G@@A^KA=_'^@@JMR#@A^-H8@@@]*[S@@@*SDFF*@I@@@@      SUBROUTINE NIDCR1(F,A,B,SE
)@@G@@AERR,RERR,LEVEL,ERROR,IFLAG,CADRE)        DCR10010    @E@@@@C  THIS FUNCSF
)@@G@@TION RETURNS AN ESTIMATE *CADRE* FOR THE NUMBER @C@@@@C     INT = INTEGRSG
)@@G@@AL OF *F*(X) FROM *A* TO *B*  @ @@@@C  WHICH HOPEFULLY SATISFIES  @G@@@@SH
)@@G@@C     ABS(INT - *CADRE*)  .LE.  AMAX1(*AERR*, *RERR* TIMES ABS(INT)).   SI
)@@G@@@F@@@@C     THE PROGRAM USES CAUTIOUS ADAPTIVE ROMBERG EXTRAPOLATION.   SJ
)@@G@@@G@@@@C  IN THIS SCHEME, THE INTEGRAL IS CALCULATED AS THE SUM OF INTEGRSK
)@@G@@ALS   @G@@@@C  OVER SUITABLY SMALL SUBINTERVALS. ON EACH SUBINTERVAL, ANSL
)@@G@@ ESTIMATE   @G@@@@C  *VINT*, WITH ESTIMATED ABSOLUTE ERROR *ERRER*, IS FSM
)@@G@@OUND BY CAUTIOUS  @G@@@@C  ROMBERG EXTRAPOLATION. IF *ERRER* IS SMALL ENSN
)@@G@@OUGH, *VINT* IS ACCEPT  @G@@@@C  ED AND ADDED TO *CADRE*, AND *ERRER* ISSO
)@@G@@ ADDED TO *ERROR*. OTHERWISE  @G@@@@C  THE SUBINTERVAL IS HALVED, AND EASP
)@@G@@CH HALF IS CONSIDERED SEPARATELY,   @F@@@@C  INFORMATION ABOUT THE OTHERSQ
)@@G@@ HALF BEING TEMPORARILY STACKED.    @[@@@@C     @B@@@@C                 SR
)@@G@@  *****   INPUT   ***** @[@@@@C     @F@@@@C  F       THE NAME OF A SINGLSS
)@@G@@E-ARGUMENT REAL FUNCTION SUBPROGRAM @F@@@@C          THIS NAME MUST APPEST
)@@G@@AR IN THE CALLING PROGRAM IN AN     @ @@@@C          EXTERNAL STATEMENT.SU
)@@G@@@E@@@@C  A,B     THE TWO ENDPOINTS OF THE INTERVAL OF INTEGRATION @]@@@@SV
)@@G@@C  AERR     @E@@@@C  RERR    DESIRED ABSOLUTE AND RELATIVE ERROR IN THE SW
)@@G@@ANSWER@[@@@@C     @B@@@@C                   *****   OUTPUT  ***** @[@@@@SX
)@@G@@C     @H@@@@C  CADRE   ESTIMATE OF THE INTEGRAL                         SY
)@@G@@            DCR1  @H@@@@C  LEVEL   NUMBER OF FUNCTION CALLS             SZ
)@@G@@                        DCR1  @G@@@@C  ERROR   ESTIMATED BOUND ON THE ABTA
)@@G@@SOLUTE ERROR OF THE NUMBER *CADRE*  @F@@@@C  IFLAG   AN INTEGER BETWEEN TB
)@@G@@1 AND 5 INDICATING WHAT DIFFICULTIES@B@@@@C          WERE MET WITH# SPECTC
)@@G@@IFICALLY    @ @@@@C          = 1, ALL IS WELL,  @G@@@@C          = 2, ONTD
)@@G@@E ORE MORE SINGULARITIES WERE SUCCESSFULLY HANDLED,   @G@@@@C          =TE
)@@G@@ 3, IN SOME SUBINTERVAL(S), THE ESTIMATE *VINT* WAS ACCEPT  @G@@@@C     TF
)@@G@@          ED MERELY BECAUSE *ERRER* WAS SMALL, EVEN THOUGH NO     @D@@@@TG
)@@G@@C               REGULAR BEHAVIOUR COULD BE RECOGNIZED,@G@@@@C          =TH
)@@G@@ 4, FAILURE, OVERFLOW OF STACK *TS* (THIS HAS NEVER HAPPEN  @A@@@@C     TI
)@@G@@          ED,  - SO FAR),     @G@@@@C          = 5, FAILURE, TOO SMALL ATJ
)@@G@@ SUBINTERVAL IS REQUIRED# THIS MAY  @G@@@@C               BE DUE TO TOO TK
)@@G@@MUCH NOISE IN THE FUNCTION (RELATIVE TO   @G@@@@C               THE GIVETL
)@@G@@N ERROR REQUIREMENTS) OR DUE TO A PLAIN ORNERY  @ @@@@C               INTM
)@@G@@TEGRAND.    @G@@@@C  A VERY CAUTIOUS MAN WOULD ACCEPT *CADRE* ONLY IF IFTN
)@@G@@LAG IS 1 OR 2#    @G@@@@C  THE MERELY REASONABLE MAN WOULD KEEP THE FAITTO
)@@G@@H EVEN IF IFLAG IS 3.   @F@@@@C  THE ADVENTUROUS MAN IS QUITE OFTEN RIGHTP
)@@G@@T IN ACCEPTING *CADRE*  @ @@@@C  EVEN IF IFLAG  IS 4 OR 5.  @[@@@@C     TQ
)@@G@@@C@@@@C     *****   LIST OF MAJOR VARIABLES   *****   @[@@@@C     @A@@@@TR
)@@G@@C  CUREST  BEST ESTIMATE SO FAR FOR @G@@@@C             INT - (INTEGRAL TS
)@@G@@OVER CURRENTLY CONSIDERED SUBINTERVAL).   @E@@@@C  FNSIZE  MAXIMUM AVERATT
)@@G@@GE FUNCTION SIZE SO FAR ENCOUNTERED,@G@@@@C  ERRR    RELATIVE ERROR REQUTU
)@@G@@IREMENT USED# DERIVED FROM INPUT *RERR*   @F@@@@C          AND CHOSEN TOTV
)@@G@@ LIE BETWEEN .1 AND 10 TIMES *TOLMCH*,    @^@@@@C  ERRA    = ABS(*AERR*)TW
)@@G@@@E@@@@C  STAGE   (MORE OR LESS) EQUAL TO 2 TO THE -(*ISTAGE*)     @G@@@@TX
)@@G@@C  THESE FIVE QUANTITIES ARE USED IN THE DETERMINATION OF THE LOCAL     TY
)@@G@@@^@@@@C  ERROR REQUIREMENT.   @[@@@@C     @C@@@@C  STEPMN  MINIMUM SUBINTZ
)@@G@@TERVAL LENGTH PERMITTED,@F@@@@C  TS      STACK OF VALUES OF F(X) SO FAR UA
)@@G@@COMPUTED BUT NOT YET    @ @@@@C          SUCCESSFULLY USED, @G@@@@C  ISTUB
)@@G@@AGE  AN INTEGER INDICATING THE HEIGHT OF THE STACK OF INTERVALS   @A@@@@UC
)@@G@@C          YET TO BE PROCESSED.     @[@@@@C     @B@@@@C     *****   LISTUD
)@@G@@ OF PARAMETERS   *****  @[@@@@C     @G@@@@C  TOLMCH  DEPENDS ON THE LENGUE
)@@G@@TH OF FLOATING POINT MANTISSA# SHOULD BE  @D@@@@C          ABOUT 1.E-7 FUF
)@@G@@OR 27 BINARY BIT MANTISSA AND @D@@@@C          ABOUT 1.E-13 FOR 48 BINARUG

)@@G@@@H@@@@      LEVEL= LEVEL + 1                                            CQ
)@@G@@      DCR1  @E@@@@      DIFF = ABS(F(BEG+RN(I)*STEP) - FBEG2-RN(I)*SLOPECR
)@@G@@)     @C@@@@      IF (DIFF .GT. TABTLM)            GO TO 72 @#@@@@   61 CS
)@@G@@CONTINUE    @C@@@@                                       GO TO 80 @G@@@@CT
)@@G@@C---------------------------------------------------------------------  CU
)@@G@@@G@@@@C------  NOISE MAY BE DOMINANT FEATURE  --------------------------CV
)@@G@@----  @F@@@@C  ESTIMATE NOISE LEVEL BY COMPARING THE VALUE OF THE INTEGRCW
)@@G@@AND AT@G@@@@C  FOUR 'RANDOMLY CHOSEN' POINTS WITH THE VALUE OF THE STRAICX
)@@G@@GHT LINE    @F@@@@C  INTERPOLATING THE INTEGRAND AT THE TWO ENDPOINTS. ICY
)@@G@@F SMALL     @ @@@@C  ENOUGH, ACCEPT *VINT*.     @ @@@@   70 SLOPE = (FENCZ
)@@G@@D-FBEG)*2.  @^@@@@      FBEG2 = FBEG*2.   @]@@@@      I = 1 @E@@@@   71 DA
)@@G@@DIFF = ABS(F(BEG+RN(I)*STEP) - FBEG2-RN(I)*SLOPE)     @H@@@@      LEVEL=DB
)@@G@@ LEVEL + 1                                                  DCR1  @B@@@@DC
)@@G@@   72 ERRER = AMAX1(ERRER,ASTEP*DIFF)     @C@@@@      IF (ERRER .GT. ERGDD
)@@G@@OAL)           GO TO 91 @#@@@@      I = I+1     @C@@@@      IF (I .LE. 4DE
)@@G@@)                    GO TO 71 @#@@@@      IFLAG = 3   @G@@@@C-----------DF
)@@G@@----------------------------------------------------------  @G@@@@C--- IDG
)@@G@@NTEGRATION OVER CURRENT SUBINTERVAL SUCCESSFUL -----------------  @F@@@@DH
)@@G@@C  ADD *VINT* TO *CADRE* AND *ERRER* TO *ERROR*, THEN SET UP NEXT @^@@@@DI
)@@G@@C  SUBINTERVAL, IF ANY. @ @@@@   80 CADRE = CADRE + VINT    @ @@@@      DJ
)@@G@@ERROR = ERROR + ERRER   @[@@@@C     @C@@@@   83 IF (RIGHT)              DK
)@@G@@         GO TO 85 @ @@@@      ISTAGE = ISTAGE - 1     @C@@@@      IF (ISDL
)@@G@@TAGE .EQ. 0)               RETURN   @[@@@@C     @ @@@@      REGLAR = REGDM
)@@G@@LSV(ISTAGE) @ @@@@      BEG = BEGIN(ISTAGE)     @ @@@@      END = FINIS(DN
)@@G@@ISTAGE)     @C@@@@      CUREST = CUREST - EST(ISTAGE+1) + VINT    @^@@@@DO
)@@G@@      IEND = IBEG - 1   @^@@@@      FEND = TS(IEND)   @ @@@@      IBEG =DP
)@@G@@ IBEGS(ISTAGE)    @C@@@@                                       GO TO 94 DQ
)@@G@@@ @@@@   85 CUREST = CUREST + VINT  @^@@@@      STAGE = STAGE*2.  @#@@@@DR
)@@G@@      IEND = IBEG @ @@@@      IBEG = IBEGS(ISTAGE)    @#@@@@      END = DS
)@@G@@BEG   @ @@@@      BEG = BEGIN(ISTAGE)     @#@@@@      FEND = FBEG @^@@@@DT
)@@G@@      FBEG = TS(IBEG)   @C@@@@                                       GO DU
)@@G@@TO 5  @G@@@@C-----------------------------------------------------------DV
)@@G@@----------  @G@@@@C--- INTEGRATION OVER CURRENT SUBINTERVAL IS UNSUCCESSDW
)@@G@@FUL-------------  @G@@@@C  MARK SUBINTERVAL FOR FURTHER SUBDIVISION. SETDX
)@@G@@ UP NEXT SUBINTERVAL.   @^@@@@   90 REGLAR = .TRUE.   @C@@@@   91 IF (ISDY
)@@G@@TAGE .EQ. MXSTGE)          GO TO 950@C@@@@   93 IF (RIGHT)              DZ
)@@G@@         GO TO 95 @A@@@@      REGLSV(ISTAGE+1) = REGLAR     @ @@@@      EA
)@@G@@BEGIN(ISTAGE) = BEG     @ @@@@      IBEGS(ISTAGE) = IBEG    @^@@@@      EB
)@@G@@STAGE = STAGE/2.  @^@@@@   94 RIGHT = .TRUE.    @^@@@@      BEG = (BEG+EEC
)@@G@@ND)/2.@ @@@@      IBEG = (IBEG+IEND)/2    @ @@@@      TS(IBEG) = TS(IBEGED
)@@G@@)/2.  @^@@@@      FBEG = TS(IBEG)   @C@@@@                              EE
)@@G@@         GO TO 6  @A@@@@   95 NNLEFT = IBEG - IBEGS(ISTAGE) @C@@@@      EF
)@@G@@IF (IEND+NNLEFT .GE. MAXTS)      GO TO 900@ @@@@      III = IBEGS(ISTAGEEG
)@@G@@)     @#@@@@      II = IEND   @^@@@@      DO 96 I=III,IBEG  @#@@@@      EH
)@@G@@II = II + 1 @^@@@@   96 TS(II) = TS(I)    @^@@@@      DO 97 I=IBEG,II   EI
)@@G@@@^@@@@      TS(III) = TS(I)   @^@@@@   97 III = III + 1     @^@@@@      EJ
)@@G@@IEND = IEND + 1   @ @@@@      IBEG = IEND - NNLEFT    @#@@@@      FEND =EK
)@@G@@ FBEG @^@@@@      FBEG = TS(IBEG)   @ @@@@      FINIS(ISTAGE) = END     EL
)@@G@@@#@@@@      END = BEG   @ @@@@      BEG = BEGIN(ISTAGE)     @ @@@@      EM
)@@G@@BEGIN(ISTAGE) = END     @ @@@@      REGLSV(ISTAGE) = REGLAR @ @@@@      EN
)@@G@@ISTAGE = ISTAGE + 1     @ @@@@      REGLAR = REGLSV(ISTAGE) @^@@@@      EO
)@@G@@EST(ISTAGE) = VINT@A@@@@      CUREST = CUREST + EST(ISTAGE) @C@@@@      EP
)@@G@@                                 GO TO 5  @G@@@@C-----------------------EQ
)@@G@@----------------------------------------------  @G@@@@C--- FAILURE TO HAER
)@@G@@NDLE GIVEN INTEGRATION PROBLEM----------------------  @#@@@@  900 IFLAG ES
)@@G@@= 4   @C@@@@                                       GO TO 999@#@@@@  950 ET
)@@G@@IFLAG = 5   @ @@@@  999 CADRE = CUREST + VINT   @C@@@@                  EU
)@@G@@                     RETURN   @]@@@@      END   ___@@@C     @C@@@@   83 EV
)@@G@@IF (RIGHT)                       GO TO 85 @ @@@@      ISTAGE = ISTAGE - EW
)@@G@@1     @C@@@@      IF (ISTAGE .EQ. 0)            )=<@)@@@@@@@)=@@C@)=$@S@EX

)@@G@@*[S@@@*SDFF*@I@@@@      SUBROUTINE NIMRAS (N, F, G, U, EPS, NSEC, IOPT, JP
)@@G@@S, IS, VINT,      MRAS0010    @I@@@@     * IOUT, $)                     JQ
)@@G@@                                    MRAS0020    @I@@@@      EXTERNAL F, JR
)@@G@@G, U                                                  MRAS0030    @I@@@@JS
)@@G@@      DIMENSION S(IS), ITEXT(3,3), ITAB(5)                              JT
)@@G@@MRAS0040    @I@@@@C     ************************************************JU
)@@G@@******************MRAS0050    @I@@@@C     NUMERICAL INTEGRATION OVER GENJV
)@@G@@ERAL REGION OF UP TO 10 DIMENSIONS. MRAS0060    @I@@@@C     IN TERMS OF JW
)@@G@@FORTRAN FUNCTIONS, THE PROBLEM SOLVED IS              MRAS0070    @I@@@@JX
)@@G@@C                                                                       JY
)@@G@@MRAS0080    @I@@@@C        *** G(1,X)   *** G(2,X)          *** G(N,X)  JZ
)@@G@@                  MRAS0090    @I@@@@C        *            *             KA
)@@G@@      *                             MRAS0100    @I@@@@C        *        KB
)@@G@@    *                   *                             MRAS0110    @I@@@@KC
)@@G@@C        *            *          . . .    *      U(X) DX1 DX2 ... DXN.  KD
)@@G@@MRAS0120    @I@@@@C        *            *                   *           KE
)@@G@@                  MRAS0130    @I@@@@C        *            *             KF
)@@G@@      *                             MRAS0140    @I@@@@C      *** F(1,X) KG
)@@G@@  *** F(2,X)          *** F(N,X)                      MRAS0150    @I@@@@KH
)@@G@@C                                                                       KI
)@@G@@MRAS0160    @I@@@@C     NIMRAS USES REPEATED APPLICATION OF SIMPSON'S RUKJ
)@@G@@LE AND ERROR      MRAS0170    @I@@@@C     CONTROL IS USED TO MAINTAIN THKK
)@@G@@E ESTIMATED TRUNCATION ERROR BELOW  MRAS0180    @I@@@@C     A USER-SPECIKL
)@@G@@FIED BOUND, EPS.  THE CODE IS A MODIFICATION OF       MRAS0190    @I@@@@KM
)@@G@@C     THE ROUTINE 'NIMDQD'.                                             KN
)@@G@@MRAS0200    @I@@@@C     ************************************************KO
)@@G@@******************MRAS0210    @I@@@@C     N      = DIMENSIONALITY.      KP
)@@G@@                                    MRAS0220    @I@@@@C     F      = FUNKQ
)@@G@@CTION SPECIFYING LOWER LIMITS OF INTEGRATION.         MRAS0230    @I@@@@KR
)@@G@@C     G      = FUNCTION SPECIFYING UPPER LIMITS OF INTEGRATION.         KS
)@@G@@MRAS0240    @I@@@@C     U      = FUNCTION SPECIFYING THE INTEGRAND.     KT
)@@G@@                  MRAS0250    @I@@@@C     EPS    = BOUND FOR ESTIMATED TKU
)@@G@@RUNCATION ERROR.                    MRAS0260    @I@@@@C     NSEC   = TIMKV
)@@G@@E LIMIT IN SECONDS.                                   MRAS0270    @I@@@@KW
)@@G@@C     IOPT   = PRINT OPTION.                                            KX
)@@G@@MRAS0280    @I@@[@C              =-1... SUPPRESS RESULTS AND WARNINGS DUKY
)@@G@@RING COMPUTATION  MRAS0285    @I@@[@C              = 0... SUPPRESS RESULKZ
)@@G@@TS AND PRINT WARNINGS DURING COMP.  MRAS0290    @I@@[@C              = 1LA
)@@G@@... PRINT RESULTS AND WARNINGS DURING COMPUTATION     MRAS0300    @I]@@@LB
)@@G@@C     S      = STORAGE ARRAY (RECOMMEND AT LEAST 500*N WORDS).          LC
)@@G@@MRAS0310    @I@@@@C     IS     = NUMBER OF WORDS IN S AVAILABLE FOR USE.LD
)@@G@@                  MRAS0320    @I@@@@C     VINT   = COMPUTED ESTIMATE OF LE
)@@G@@INTEGRAL.                           MRAS0330    @I@@@@C     IOUT   = STALF
)@@G@@TUS CODE.                                             MRAS0340    @I@@@@LG
)@@G@@C              =1 ... O.K. (NO WARNINGS OR ERRORS IN COMPUTATION).      LH
)@@G@@MRAS0350    @I@@@@C              =2 ... O.K. BUT NIMRAS HAD TO CHANGE TOLI
)@@G@@ UNIFORM STEP     MRAS0360    @I@@@@C                     ALGORITHM WHICLJ
)@@G@@H SLOWED COMPUTATION.               MRAS0370    @I@@@@C              =3 LK
)@@G@@... G<F OCCURED AND G=F WAS ASSUMED AT SOME POINTS.   MRAS0380    @I@@@@LL
)@@G@@C                     CHECK INTEGRAND AND LIMITS.                       LM
)@@G@@MRAS0390    @I@@@@C              =4 ... NO GOOD, INTEGRATION STEP UNDERFLN
)@@G@@LOW OCCURED.      MRAS0400    @I@@@@C              =5 ... NO GOOD, TIME LO
)@@G@@LIMIT REACHED.                      MRAS0410    @I@@@@C              =6 LP
)@@G@@... NO GOOD, ERRORS IN CALLING SEQUENCE DETECTED.     MRAS0420    @I@@@@LQ
)@@G@@C     $K     = RETURN TO STATEMENT K IF NO GOOD (IOUT EXCEEDS 3).       LR
)@@G@@MRAS0430    @I@@@@C     ************************************************LS
)@@G@@******************MRAS0440    @I@@@@      DATA NCALL, ITAB, ITEXT /0, 2,LT
)@@G@@ 2, 3, 1, 1,                        MRAS0450    @I@@@@     *'   INTEGRATLU
)@@G@@ION NOT','    INTEGRATION IS','INTEGRATION MAY BE'/   MRAS0460    @I@@@@LV
)@@G@@      T0= TIMEF(0.)                                                     LW
)@@G@@MRAS0470    @I@@@@      NCALL= NCALL + 1                                LX
)@@G@@                  MRAS0480    @I@@@@C     CHECK NO. PARAMETERS.         LY
)@@G@@                                    MRAS0490    @I@@@@      CALL URXITP LZ
)@@G@@(12)                                                  MRAS0500    @I@@@@MA
)@@G@@C     CHECK FOR WARNINGS AND ERRORS.                                    MB
)@@G@@MRAS0510    @I@@@@      IOUT= 0                                         MC
)@@G@@                  MRAS0520    @I@@@@C     CHECK IF F, G, U ARE FUNCTIONSMD
)@@G@@.                                   MRAS0530    @I@@@@      INCODE= FLD(ME
)@@G@@0,6,F)                                                MRAS0540    @I@@@@MF
)@@G@@      IF (INCODE .EQ. 0 .OR. INCODE .EQ. 63) CALL NIXERR (6, 'F', IOUT) MG
)@@G@@MRAS0550    @I@@@@      INCODE= FLD (0,6,G)                             MH
)@@G@@                  MRAS0560    @I@@@@      IF (INCODE .EQ. 0 .OR. INCODE MI
)@@G@@.EQ. 63) CALL NIXERR (6, 'G', IOUT) MRAS0570    @I@@@@      INCODE= FLD(MJ
)@@G@@0,6,U)                                                MRAS0580    @I@@@@MK
)@@G@@      IF (INCODE .EQ. 0 .OR. INCODE .EQ. 63) CALL NIXERR (6, 'U', IOUT) ML
)@@G@@MRAS0590    @I@@@@C     CHECK N, EPS, NSEC, IS.                         MM
)@@G@@                  MRAS0600    @I@@@@      IF (N .LT. 1 .OR. N .GT. 10) CMN
)@@G@@ALL NIXERR (7, N, IOUT)             MRAS0610    @I@@@@      IF (EPS .LE.MO
)@@G@@ 0.0) CALL NIXERR (8, EPS, IOUT)                      MRAS0620    @I@@@@MP
)@@G@@      IF (NSEC .LT. 1 .AND. NSEC .NE. 'NONE') CALL NIXERR (9,NSEC, IOUT)MQ
)@@G@@MRAS0630    @I@@@@      IF (IS .LT. 5*N) CALL NIXERR (10, IS, IOUT)     MR
)@@G@@                  MRAS0640    @I@@@@C     CHECK IOPT (DEFAULT=1)        MS
)@@G@@                                    MRAS0650    @I@@[@      IF (ABS(IOPTMT
)@@G@@) .GT. 1) CALL NIXERR (1, IOPT, IOUT)                 MRAS0660    @I[@@@MU
)@@G@@      IF (IOUT .EQ. 1) CALL URWALK ('NIMRAS', 0)                        MV
)@@G@@MRAS0680    @I@@@@C     TERMINATE IF ERRORS OCCURED.                    MW
)@@G@@                  MRAS0700    @I@@@@      IF (IOUT .EQ. 6) GO TO 60     MX
)@@G@@                                    MRAS0710    @I@@@@C     SOLVE USING MY
)@@G@@SECOND LEVEL ROUTINE, NIMRS1.                         MRAS0720    @I@@@@MZ
)@@G@@   20 IOUT= 1                                                           NA
)@@G@@MRAS0730    @I@@@@      NT= IS/5                                        NB
)@@G@@                  MRAS0740    @I@@@@      NC= NT/N                      NC
)@@G@@                                    MRAS0750    @I@@@@      CALL NIMRS1 ND
)@@G@@(U, F, G, N, NFEI, NFEL, EPS, VINT, NSEC, IOUT, NC,   MRAS0760    @I@@[@NE
)@@G@@     * S(1), S(NT+1), S(2 *NT+1), S(3*NT+1), S(4*NT+1), IOPT)           NF
)@@G@@MRAS0770    @I[@@@C     PRINT RESULTS IF REQUESTED.                     NG
)@@G@@                  MRAS0780    @I@@[@      IF (IOPT .EQ. 0 .OR. IOPT .EQ.NH
)@@G@@ -1) GO TO 50                       MRAS0790    @I[@@@   30 T1= .001*(TINI
)@@G@@MEF(1.) - T0)                                         MRAS0800    @I@@@@NJ
)@@G@@      MSG= ITAB(IOUT)                                                   NK
)@@G@@MRAS0810    @I@@@@      NFETOT= NFEI + NFEL                             NL
)@@G@@                  MRAS0820    @I@@@@      PRINT 40, NCALL, N, (ITEXT(I,MNM
)@@G@@SG), I= 1, 3), IOUT, NFEI, NFEL,    MRAS0830    @I@@@@     * NFETOT, VINNN
)@@G@@T, T1                                                 MRAS0840    @I@@@@NO
)@@G@@   40 FORMAT (1H0, 12(6H******) / 1H ,'NIMRAS CALL NO.', I4,            NP
)@@G@@MRAS0850    @I@@@@     * ',   INTEGRATION OVER REGION IN', I2, '-DIMENSINQ
)@@G@@ONAL SPACE' /     MRAS0860    @I@@@@     * 1H0, 3X, 3A6, ' SUCCESSFUL, SNR
)@@G@@TATUS CODE =', I3 /                 MRAS0870    @I@@@@     * 1H0, 5X, 'NNS
)@@G@@UMBER OF', 14X, 'INTEGRAND', 8X, 'LIMITS', 9X,        MRAS0880    @I@@@@NT
)@@G@@     * 'TOTAL' / 1H , 'FUNCTION EVALUATIONS', 3I15 / 1H0,               NU
)@@G@@MRAS0890    @I@@@@     * 'INTEGRAL VALUE =', G15.8, 5X, 'COMPUTATION TIMNV
)@@G@@E =', F8.3,       MRAS0900    @I@@@@     * ' SECONDS' / 1H , 12(6H******NW
)@@G@@) /)                                MRAS0910    @I@@@@   50 IF (IOUT .LENX
)@@G@@. 3) RETURN                                           MRAS0920    @I@@@@NY
)@@G@@C     ERROR RETURN.                                                     NZ
)@@G@@MRAS0930    @I@@@@   60 CALL URTRET (12, JERR)                          OA
)@@G@@                  MRAS0940    @I@@@@      IF (JERR) 80, 80, 70          OB
)@@G@@                                    MRAS0950    @I@@@@   70 IF (IOUT .EQOC
)@@G@@. 6) CALL URWALK ('NIMRAS', 0)                        MRAS0960    @I@@@@OD
)@@G@@      RETURN 12                                                         OE
)@@G@@MRAS0970    @I@@@@   80 CALL NIXERR (11, 0, JERR)                       OF
)@@G@@                  MRAS0975    @I@@@@      CALL URWALK ('NIMRAS', 1)     OG
)@@G@@                                    MRAS0978    @I@@@@      RETURN      OH
)@@G@@                                                      MRAS0980    @I@@@@OI
)@@G@@      END                                                               OJ
)@@G@@MRAS0990    ___VE USING SECOND LEVEL ROUTINE, NIMRS1.                   OK

)@@G@@SUBROUTINE NIMRS1 (U, F, G, N, NFEI, NFEL, EPSMAX, VALUE, NSEC,   @B@@@@VQ
)@@G@@     * IOUT, NC, A, I, F1, F2, F3, IOPT)  @^@@@@      EXTERNAL F, G, U  VR
)@@G@@@ @@@@C********* VARIABLE WORKSPACE @E@@@@      DIMENSION A(N,NC),I(N,NCVS
)@@G@@),F1(N,NC),F2(N,NC),F3(N,NC)  @ @@@@C********** FIXED WORKSPACE   @F@@@@VT
)@@G@@      DIMENSION V(11),H(10),X(10),KK(10),LENGTH(10),SUM1(10),     @C@@@@VU
)@@G@@     *           SUM2(10),SUM3(10),JTAB(10),    @G@@@@     *           EVV
)@@G@@PS(10),J(10),M(10),MSTART(10),JEND(10),K(10),P(10),   @C@@@@     *      VW
)@@G@@     LL(10),      FA(10),FB(10)     @B@@@@      EQUIVALENCE (FA,SUM2),(FVX
)@@G@@B,SUM3)     @ @@@@      REAL I,LENGTH,I1,I2     @^@@@@C********** INITIAVY
)@@G@@LIZE  @^@@@@      TIMLST=URTIMG(0)  @ @@@@       TIMEND=TIMLST+NSEC     VZ
)@@G@@@#@@@@       MAXCNT=10  @#@@@@       NCOUNT=10  @ @@@@       EOVN15=EPSMWA
)@@G@@AX/N*15.    @#@@@@      NFEI= 0     @#@@@@      NFEL= 2     @B@[@@C     WB
)@@G@@CHECK IF WARNINGS SHOULD BE PRINTED @#@[@@      IWARN= 0    @A@[@@      WC
)@@G@@IF (IOPT .EQ. -1) IWARN= 10   @^@[@@      NCODE2= IWARN     @^@[@@      WD
)@@G@@NCODE3= IWARN     @#@]@[      NCODE2= 0   @#@]@[      NCODE3= 0   @]@@[]WE
)@@G@@      LW= 0 @ @@[]      IF (IOPT .EQ. -1) LW= 9 @#@@[]      NCODE2= LW  WF
)@@G@@@#@@[]      NCODE3= LW  @^]@@@      A(1,1)= F(1,X)    @A@@@@      LENGTHWG
)@@G@@(1)= G(1,X) - A(1,1)    @]@@@@      L=1   @#@@@@      GO TO 60    @ @@@@WH
)@@G@@C********** GO DOWN A LEVEL   @]@@@@ 50   L=L+1 @^@@@@      NFEL= NFEL +WI
)@@G@@ 2    @^@@@@      A(L,1)= F(L,X)    @A@@@@      LENGTH(L)= G(L,X) - A(L,WJ
)@@G@@1)    @]@@@@ 60   V(L)=0@ @@@@      IF(LENGTH(L))62,2000,65 @A@@@@   62 WK
)@@G@@IF (NCODE3 .EQ. 10) GO TO 2000@ @[@@      CALL NIXERR (3, L, IOUT)@]@@@[WL
)@@G@@      LW= L @ @@@[      IF (IOPT .EQ. -1) LW= -1@A@@@[      CALL NIXERR WM
)@@G@@(3, LW, IOUT)     @D@@@@      IF (NCODE3 .EQ. 0) CALL URWALK ('NIMRS1', WN
)@@G@@0)    @D@[@@      IF (NCODE3 .EQ. 9) CALL NIXERR (0, 0, IOUT)     @D@@@[WO
)@@G@@      IF (NCODE3 .EQ. 9) CALL NIXERR (0, IOPT, IOUT)  @A@@@@C     MAXIMUWP
)@@G@@M OF 10 MESSAGES OUTPUT @^@@@@      NCODE3= NCODE3 + 1@#@@@@      GO TO WQ
)@@G@@2000  @#@@@@ 65     JTAB(L)=1 @^@@@@      H(L)=.5*LENGTH(L) @^@@@@      WR
)@@G@@ EPS(L)=EOVN15    @#@@@@      LM1 = L - 1 @ @@@@       IF(LM1 .EQ. 0) GOWS
)@@G@@ TO 75@ @@@@      DO 70 INDEX = 1,LM1     @A@@@@ 70   EPS(L)=EPS(L)/LENGWT
)@@G@@TH(INDEX)   @#@@@@ 75   X(L)=A(L,1) @#@@@@      K(L)=-1     @]@@@@      WU
)@@G@@J(L)=1@#@@@@       M(L)=NC    @^@@@@       MSTART(L)=NC     @#@@@@      WV
)@@G@@JEND(L)=0   @^@@@@ 100  IF(L.NE.N)GO TO 50@B@@@@C********** BEGIN -- TIMWW
)@@G@@E CHECK SECTION   @B@@@@      IF (NSEC .EQ. 'NONE') GO TO 200     @^@@@@WX
)@@G@@       NCOUNT = NCOUNT-1@A@@@@       IF(NCOUNT .NE. 0) GO TO 200  @#@@@@WY
)@@G@@       TIME=TIMLST@ @@@@         TIMLST=URTIMG(0)     @^@@@@       TIME=WZ
)@@G@@TIMLST-TIME @A@@@@       IF(TIME .GT. 0) GO TO 140    @ @@@@       MAXCNXA
)@@G@@T=MAXCNT*1000     @^@@@@       NCOUNT=MAXCNT    @#@@@@       GO TO 200  XB
)@@G@@@B@@@@ 140   IF(TIMLST.GT.TIMEND) GO TO 5000    @B@@@@       NCOUNT=MAX(XC
)@@G@@INT(MAXCNT/TIME+.5),1)  @B@@@@C********** END -- TIME CHECK SECTION     XD
)@@G@@@#@@@@ 200  V(L+1)=U(X) @^@@@@      NFEI= NFEI + 1    @#@@@@       NGO=JXE
)@@G@@TAB(L)@C@@@@       GO TO (500,600,700,1100,1200,3100),NGO   @^@@@@ 500  XF
)@@G@@F1(L,1)=V(L+1)    @^@@@@      X(L)=A(L,1) + H(L)@#@@@@       JTAB(L)=2  XG
)@@G@@@#@@@@      GO TO 100   @^@@@@ 600  F2(L,1) = V(L+1)  @ @@@@      X(L)=AXH
)@@G@@(L,1) + LENGTH(L) @#@@@@       JTAB(L)=3  @#@@@@      GO TO 100   @^@@@@XI
)@@G@@ 700  F3(L,1)=V(L+1)    @E@@@@      I(L,1)=LENGTH(L)/6.*(F1(L,1) + 4.*F2XJ
)@@G@@(L,1) + F3(L,1))  @#@@@@      GO TO 1050  @ @@@@C********** VARIABLE STEXK
)@@G@@P     @^@@@@ 1000 EPS(L) = .5*EPS(L)@^@@@@      H(L) = .5*H(L)    @A@@@@XL
)@@G@@      IF(H(L) .LE. 0.0)GO TO 5010   @A@@@@ 1050 IF(J(L).EQ.JEND(L))GO TOXM
)@@G@@ 1800 @#@@@@       NN=J(L)    @ @@@@       X(L)=A(L,NN) + .5*H(L) @#@@@@XN
)@@G@@       JTAB(L)=4  @#@@@@      GO TO 100   @#@@@@ 1100 FA(L)=V(L+1)@#@@@@XO
)@@G@@       NN=J(L)    @ @@@@       X(L)=A(L,NN) + 1.5*H(L)@#@@@@       JTAB(XP
)@@G@@L)=5  @#@@@@      GO TO 100   @#@@@@ 1200 FB(L)=V(L+1)@#@@@@      J1=J(LXQ
)@@G@@)     @#@@@@      HO6=H(L)/6. @C@@@@      I1=HO6*(F1(L,J1) + 4.*FA(L) + XR
)@@G@@F2(L,J1))   @C@@@@      I2=HO6*(F2(L,J1) + 4.*FB(L) + F3(L,J1))   @ @@@@XS
)@@G@@      ERR = I1+I2-I(L,J1)     @B@@@@      IF(ABS (ERR).LT.EPS(L))GO TO 1XT
)@@G@@500   @ @@@@      IF(M(L).EQ.J1)GO TO 3000@#@@@@      M1=M(L)     @^@@@@XU
)@@G@@      M2=M(L) + K(L)    @^@@@@      A(L,M1)=A(L,J1)   @ @@@@      A(L,M2XV
)@@G@@) =A(L,J1) + H(L) @#@@@@      I(L,M1)=I1  @#@@@@      I(L,M2)=I2  @^@@@@XW
)@@G@@      F1(L,M1)=F1(L,J1) @^@@@@      F2(L,M1)=FA(L)    @^@@@@       F3(L,XX
)@@G@@M1)=F2(L,J1)@^@@@@       F1(L,M2)=F2(L,J1)@^@@@@      F2(L,M2)=FB(L)    XY
)@@G@@@^@@@@      F3(L,M2)=F3(L,J1) @^@@@@      M(L) = M2 + K(L)  @^@@@@      XZ
)@@G@@J(L)=J(L) + K(L)  @#@@@@      GO TO 1050  @B@@@@ 1500 V(L) = ERR/15. + IYA
)@@G@@1 + I2 + V(L)     @^@@@@      J(L)=J(L) + K(L)  @#@@@@      GO TO 1050  YB
)@@G@@@B@@@@ 1800 IF(M(L).EQ.MSTART(L))GO TO 2000     @ @@@@      IF(K(L))1900YC
)@@G@@,1900,1950  @]@@@@ 1900 K(L)=1@^@@@@      J(L)=M(L) + 1     @^@@@@      YD
)@@G@@JEND(L)=NC + 1    @#@@@@       M(L)=1     @#@@@@       MSTART(L)=1@#@@@@YE
)@@G@@      GO TO 1000  @#@@@@ 1950 K(L)=-1     @^@@@@      J(L)=M(L) - 1     YF
)@@G@@@#@@@@      JEND(L)=0   @^@@@@       MSTART(L)=NC     @#@@@@       M(L)=YG
)@@G@@NC    @#@@@@      GO TO 1000  @ @@@@C********** GO UP A LEVEL     @#@@@@YH
)@@G@@ 2000 L=L - 1     @ @@@@      IF(L.EQ.0)GO TO 2100    @#@@@@       NGO=JYI
)@@G@@TAB(L)@C@@@@       GO TO (500,600,700,1100,1200,3100),NGO   @#@@@@ 2100 YJ
)@@G@@VALUE=V(1)  @]@@@@      RETURN@^@@@@C********** UNIFORM STEP@A@@@@ 3000 YK
)@@G@@IF (NCODE2 .EQ. 10) GO TO 3025@ @[@@      CALL NIXERR (2, 0, IOUT)@A@@@[YL
)@@G@@      CALL NIXERR (2, IOPT, IOUT)   @D@@@@      IF (NCODE2 .EQ. 0) CALL YM
)@@G@@URWALK ('NIMRS1', 0)    @D@[@@      IF (NCODE2 .EQ. 9) CALL NIXERR (0, 0YN
)@@G@@, IOUT)     @D@@@[      IF (NCODE2 .EQ. 9) CALL NIXERR (0, IOPT, IOUT)  YO
)@@G@@@A@@@@C     MAXIMUM OF 10 MESSAGES OUTPUT @^@@@@      NCODE2= NCODE2 + 1YP
)@@G@@@A@@@@ 3025 SUM1(L) = F1(L,J1) + F3(L,J1) @B@@@@      SUM2(L)=FA(L) + F2YQ
)@@G@@(L,J1)+ FB(L)     @#@@@@C*** SAVE H(L)    @^@@@@      F1(L,J1) = H(L)   YR
)@@G@@@#@@@@      H(L)=.5*H(L)@ @@@@      IF(H(L).LE.0)GO TO 5010 @#@@@@      YS
)@@G@@KK(L)=4     @#@@@@      P(L)=I1 + I2@#@@@@ 3030 SUM3(L)=0   @ @@@@      YT
)@@G@@X(L)=A(L,J1) + .5*H(L)  @#@@@@      LL(L)=1     @A@@@@ 3050 IF(LL(L).GT.YU
)@@G@@KK(L))GO TO 3500  @#@@@@       JTAB(L)=6  @#@@@@      GO TO 100   @ @@@@YV
)@@G@@ 3100 SUM3(L)=SUM3(L) + V(L+1)@^@@@@      LL(L)=LL(L) + 1   @^@@@@      YW
)@@G@@X(L)=X(L) + H(L)  @#@@@@      GO TO 3050  @D@@@@ 3500 I2=H(L)/6.*(SUM1(LYX
)@@G@@) + 2.*SUM2(L) + 4.*SUM3(L))  @^@@@@      ERR = I2 - P(L)   @B@@@@      YY
)@@G@@IF(ABS (ERR).LT.EPS(L))GO TO 3600   @A@@@@      SUM2(L)=SUM2(L) + SUM3(LYZ
)@@G@@)     @^@@@@      KK(L)=2*KK(L)     @#@@@@      H(L)=.5*H(L)@#@@@@      ZA
)@@G@@P(L)=I2     @#@@@@      GO TO 3030  @A@@@@ 3600 V(L) = ERR/15. + I2 + V(ZB
)@@G@@L)    @#@@@@C*** RESTORE H(L) @#@@@@       NN=J(L)    @^@@@@       H(L)=ZC
)@@G@@F1(L,NN)    @^@@@@      J(L)=J(L)+K(L)    @#@@@@      GO TO 1050  @^@@@@ZD
)@@G@@C********** ERROR RETURN@A@@@@ 5000 CALL NIXERR (5, NSEC, IOUT)   @#@@@@ZE
)@@G@@      GO TO 5050  @ @@@@ 5010 CALL NIXERR (4, 0, IOUT)@A@@@@ 5050 CALL UZF
)@@G@@RWALK ('NIMRS1', 0)     @#@@@@      GO TO 2100  @]@@@@       END  ___(L,ZG
)@@G@@J1)   @ @@@@      A(L,M2)@@[N#]A[#@-)K0CS@C]@@#ZG.)__"C[)@#VG.@__"C[@@#YZH

)@@G@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@*[S@@@*SDFF*@I@@@@      SUBROUTINE NIXQDA (F, A,DB
)@@G@@ B, TOL, IOPT, VINT, ERR, IOUT, $)        NIXQ0010    @I@@@@      EXTERNDC
)@@G@@AL F                                                        NIXQ0020    DD
)@@G@@@I@@@@      DIMENSION NCALL(2), IAM(2), ITEXT(3,3), ITAB(4)             DE
)@@G@@      NIXQ0030    @I@@@@      DATA ITAB /2, 2, 3, 1/                    DF
)@@G@@                        NIXQ0035    @I@@@@      DATA NCALL, IAM, ITEXT /DG
)@@G@@2*0, 'NIXQDA', 'NIXQDB',                  NIXQ0040    @I@@@@     * '   IDH
)@@G@@NTEGRATION NOT', '    INTEGRATION IS', 'INTEGRATION MAY BE'/NIXQ0050    DI
)@@G@@@I@@@@      IALG= 1                                                     DJ
)@@G@@      NIXQ0060    @I@@@@      GO TO 10                                  DK
)@@G@@                        NIXQ0070    @I@@@@      ENTRY NIXQDB (F, A, B, TDL
)@@G@@OL, IOPT, VINT, ERR, IOUT, $)             NIXQ0080    @I@@@@      IALG= DM
)@@G@@2                                                           NIXQ0090    DN
)@@G@@@I@@@@C     ************************************************************DO
)@@G@@******NIXQ0100    @I@@@@C     NUMERICAL INTEGRATION OF F(X)DX OVER (A,B)DP
)@@G@@ USING THE OPTIMAL      NIXQ0110    @I@@@@C     EXTENSION OF THE 3-POINTDQ
)@@G@@ GAUSS RULE WHICH MAXIMIZES THE DEGREE    NIXQ0120    @I@@@@C     OF PREDR
)@@G@@CISION SUBJECT TO NO PREVIOUS FUNCTION EVALUATIONS BEING    NIXQ0130    DS
)@@G@@@I@@@@C     WASTED.  IF THE CONVERGENCE CRITERION SPECIFIED BY TOL IS NODT
)@@G@@T MET NIXQ0140    @I@@@@C     AFTER THE 255-POINT RULE IS USED, THE INTEDU
)@@G@@RVAL IS SUBDIVIDED      NIXQ0150    @I@@@@C     USING AN ADAPTIVE SUBDIVDV
)@@G@@ISION PROCESS FOR NIXQDA OR A NON-        NIXQ0160    @I@@@@C     ADAPTIDW
)@@G@@VE SUBDIVISION PROCESS FOR NIXQDB.  SOURCE... ALGORITHM 468 NIXQ0170    DX
)@@G@@@I@@@@C     COMMUNICATIONS OF THE A.C.M., NOVEMBER, 1973.               DY
)@@G@@      NIXQ0180    @I@@@@C     ******************************************DZ
)@@G@@************************NIXQ0190    @I@@@@C     F     = NAME OF FUNCTIONEA
)@@G@@ TO BE INTEGRATED                         NIXQ0200    @I@@@@C     A     EB
)@@G@@= LOWER LIMIT OF INTEGRATION                                NIXQ0210    EC
)@@G@@@I@@@@C     B     = UPPER LIMIT OF INTEGRATION                          ED
)@@G@@      NIXQ0220    @I@@@@C     TOL   = RELATIVE ACCURACY DESIRED         EE
)@@G@@                        NIXQ0230    @I@@@@C     IOPT  = OUTPUT OPTION   EF
)@@G@@                                          NIXQ0240    @I@@@@C           EG
)@@G@@= -1 ... SUPPRESS RESULTS AND WARNINGS DURING COMPUTATION   NIXQ0242    EH
